What to Do When Things Break
Problem	Solution
Friends page shows nothing	Check Section 1 Block 2 SQL ran — the follows table must exist
Banner upload fails	Check Section 1 Block 3 SQL ran — storage buckets must exist. Also confirm the bucket is public in Supabase Storage.
Spotify connect does nothing	Check Supabase Auth Providers has Spotify enabled + redirect URI matches exactly
Images still show emoji	Hard-refresh the browser (Cmd+Shift+R on Mac). The iTunes lookup is async — wait 2–3 seconds after page load.
Link preview still shows Vercel logo	og-image.png must be in /public folder. og:image URL must be absolute (https://...). Use opengraph.xyz to debug.
Nav overflows on mobile	Confirm the CSS media queries from Section 3 were appended (not replaced) in globals.css
Password not enforcing on signup	The validatePassword function must be defined before the Auth() component. Check for typos in the regex.
Red error: Module not found	A file is importing something that does not exist. Read the error — it shows exactly which import is missing.
git push rejected	Run git pull first to get any remote changes, then push again
Vercel builds but site broken	Add all new env vars to Vercel Settings → Environment Variables → redeploy

SECTION 1  —  CRITICAL FIX — NEWSBANNER.JS HAS TERMINAL COMMANDS INSIDE IT

What happened: When you ran the cat << EOF heredoc command for NewsBanner.js, the terminal commands themselves (cd ~/Desktop/banger-ratios, mkdir -p ...) got written into the file as JavaScript. Next.js tried to parse them as code and crashed.

⚠  This is why you see: cd ~/Desktop/banger-ratios on line 4 of NewsBanner.js. The fix is to completely overwrite the file with correct content. Run the Python command below — it writes the file directly without heredoc, so this cannot happen again.

Fix: Run this single Python command in terminal
Open Terminal. Make sure you are in your project folder first:
cd ~/Desktop/banger-ratios

Then run this — copy and paste the ENTIRE block at once, all the way to the last quote mark:
python3 << 'PYEOF'
content = '''
// File: src/app/components/NewsBanner.js
'use client'
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
 
const FALLBACK = [
  'Kendrick Lamar leads the leaderboard with 91% Banger Ratio',
  'Frank Ocean Blonde holds #1 — 96% community score',
  'New: follow friends and see their ratings in real time',
  'Tyler, the Creator IGOR — 93% Banger Ratio from 800+ raters',
  'Chappell Roan rises to 87% — The Rise and Fall of a Midwest Princess',
]
 
export default function NewsBanner() {
  const [headlines, setHeadlines] = useState(FALLBACK)
 
  useEffect(() => {
    const key = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_LASTFM_KEY
    if (!key) return
    fetch(`https://ws.audioscrobbler.com/2.0/?method=chart.gettoptracks&api_key=${key}&format=json&limit=10`)
      .then(r => r.json())
      .then(d => {
        const tracks = d?.tracks?.track
        if (tracks?.length) {
          setHeadlines(tracks.map(t => `${t.name} by ${t.artist.name} — trending now`))
        }
      })
      .catch(() => {})
  }, [])
 
  const text = headlines.join('  ◆  ')
 
  return (
    <div style={{ background:'var(--pink)', overflow:'hidden', height:32,
      display:'flex', alignItems:'center' }}>
      <div style={{ display:'inline-flex',
        animation:'scroll 90s linear infinite',
        whiteSpace:'nowrap' }}>
        <span style={{ color:'#fff', fontSize:'0.8rem',
          letterSpacing:'0.04em', paddingRight:80 }}>{text}</span>
        <span style={{ color:'#fff', fontSize:'0.8rem',
          letterSpacing:'0.04em', paddingRight:80 }}>{text}</span>
      </div>
      <style>{`@keyframes scroll { from { transform:translateX(0) } to { transform:translateX(-50%) } }`}</style>
    </div>
  )
}
'''
import os
os.makedirs('src/app/components', exist_ok=True)
with open('src/app/components/NewsBanner.js', 'w') as f:
    f.write(content.lstrip())
print('NewsBanner.js fixed!')

SECTION 2  —  THE PYTHON AUTOPATCHER — ONE SCRIPT, ALL EDITS

This single Python script reads your actual source files, finds the right locations automatically, and makes every edit from DEP XII and XIII without you needing to search for lines or use VS Code at all. Run it once and all changes are applied.

What the autopatcher does
albums/page.js	Injects artwork fetch state + useEffect. Replaces the 🎵 emoji at line 170 and 196 with real iTunes artwork.
artists/page.js	Injects artist image fetch. Replaces gradient avatar with real photo + fallback.
components/Nav.js	Reduces link gap to 0.75rem. Adds Settings link.
globals.css	Appends album card truncation CSS and nav spacing fix.
app/terms/page.js	Creates the Terms & Conditions page (new file).
app/settings/page.js	Creates the full Settings page (new file).
app/components/Footer.js	Creates Footer with © 2026 (new file).
app/layout.js	Adds Footer import and component to the layout.
app/friends/page.js	Rewrites with magnifying glass search button.
middleware.js	Creates rate limiting middleware for bot protection.
next.config.js	Adds security headers.

Step 1 — Save the patcher script
Copy this ENTIRE block and paste it into terminal. It saves the script file first, then you run it separately so you can inspect it before applying changes.
cd ~/Desktop/banger-ratios
 
python3 << 'PYEOF'
PATCHER = '''
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# BR DEP XIV — Banger Ratios Autopatcher
# Run from: ~/Desktop/banger-ratios
# Usage: python3 br_patcher.py
 
import os, re, sys
 
ROOT = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))
changed = []
skipped = []
errors = []
 
def read(path):
    full = os.path.join(ROOT, path)
    if not os.path.exists(full):
        return None
    with open(full) as f:
        return f.read()
 
def write(path, content):
    full = os.path.join(ROOT, path)
    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(full), exist_ok=True)
    with open(full, 'w') as f:
        f.write(content)
    changed.append(path)
    print(f'  ✓  {path}')
 
def patch(path, old, new, description=''):
    content = read(path)
    if content is None:
        errors.append(f'{path}: file not found')
        return False
    if old not in content:
        skipped.append(f'{path}: target not found — {description or old[:60]}')
        return False
    if new in content and old not in content:
        skipped.append(f'{path}: already patched')
        return False
    write(path, content.replace(old, new, 1))
    return True
 
def append_if_missing(path, content, marker):
    existing = read(path) or ''
    if marker in existing:
        skipped.append(f'{path}: {marker} already present')
        return
    full = os.path.join(ROOT, path)
    with open(full, 'a') as f:
        f.write(content)
    changed.append(path + ' (appended)')
    print(f'  ✓  {path} (appended)')
 
print('\n=== BR DEP XIV Autopatcher ===')
print('Reading your project files...\n')
 
# ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# 1. ALBUMS PAGE — inject artwork fetch
# ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
print('[ albums/page.js ]')
albums_code = read('src/app/albums/page.js')
if albums_code:
    if 'seedArtwork' not in albums_code:
        # Find first useState line
        m = re.search(r'(const \[\w+, set\w+\] = (?:React\.)?useState\([^)]*\))', albums_code)
        if m:
            inject = '''
  const [seedArtwork, setSeedArtwork] = useState({})
 
  useEffect(() => {
    async function fetchSeedArtwork() {
      const list = typeof SEED_ALBUMS !== 'undefined' ? SEED_ALBUMS : []
      const results = await Promise.all(
        list.map(async (album) => {
          try {
            const id = album.itunes_id || album.itunesId || album.id
            if (!id) return [null, null]
            const r = await fetch(`https://itunes.apple.com/lookup?id=${id}&entity=album`)
            const d = await r.json()
            const url = d.results?.[0]?.artworkUrl100?.replace('100x100', '400x400')
            return [id, url]
          } catch { return [null, null] }
        })
      )
      setSeedArtwork(Object.fromEntries(results.filter(([k,v]) => k && v)))
    }
    fetchSeedArtwork()
  }, [])'''
            albums_code = albums_code.replace(m.group(1), m.group(1) + inject, 1)
            # Also ensure useEffect is imported
            if 'useEffect' not in albums_code:
                albums_code = albums_code.replace("import { useState }", "import { useState, useEffect }")
                albums_code = albums_code.replace("import { useState,", "import { useState, useEffect,")
            write('src/app/albums/page.js', albums_code)
        else:
            errors.append('albums/page.js: no useState found — check file manually')
    else:
        skipped.append('albums/page.js: seedArtwork already present')
 
    # Replace emoji placeholders with artwork
    albums_code2 = read('src/app/albums/page.js')
    ARTWORK_JSX = '''
                  {(seedArtwork[album.itunes_id] || seedArtwork[album.itunesId] || seedArtwork[album.id])
                    ? <img
                        src={seedArtwork[album.itunes_id] || seedArtwork[album.itunesId] || seedArtwork[album.id]}
                        alt={album.title || ''}
                        style={{ width:'100%', aspectRatio:'1', objectFit:'cover',
                                 borderRadius:10, marginBottom:'1rem', display:'block' }}
                      />
                    : <div style={{ width:'100%', aspectRatio:'1', background:'#1a1a1a',
                        borderRadius:10, display:'flex', alignItems:'center',
                        justifyContent:'center', marginBottom:'1rem', fontSize:'3rem' }}>
                        \U0001F3B5
                      </div>
                  }'''
    if albums_code2:
        for old_pattern in [
            '                  }}>\U0001F3B5</div>',
            '\U0001F3B5',
        ]:
            if old_pattern in albums_code2 and 'seedArtwork' not in albums_code2[albums_code2.find(old_pattern)-200:albums_code2.find(old_pattern)]:
                albums_code2 = albums_code2.replace(old_pattern, ARTWORK_JSX, 1)
                write('src/app/albums/page.js', albums_code2)
                print('    → emoji placeholder replaced with artwork')
                break
else:
    errors.append('src/app/albums/page.js not found')
 
# ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# 2. ARTISTS PAGE — inject image fetch
# ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
print('[ artists/page.js ]')
artists_code = read('src/app/artists/page.js')
if artists_code:
    if 'artistImages' not in artists_code:
        m = re.search(r'(const \[\w+, set\w+\] = (?:React\.)?useState\([^)]*\))', artists_code)
        if m:
            inject = '''
  const [artistImages, setArtistImages] = useState({})
 
  useEffect(() => {
    async function fetchArtistImages() {
      const list = typeof FEATURED_ARTISTS !== 'undefined' ? FEATURED_ARTISTS : []
      const results = await Promise.all(
        list.map(async (artist) => {
          try {
            const id = artist.id || artist.itunes_id
            const r = await fetch(`https://itunes.apple.com/lookup?id=${id}&entity=album&limit=1`)
            const d = await r.json()
            const img = d.results?.[0]?.artworkUrl100?.replace('100x100', '300x300')
            return [id, img]
          } catch { return [null, null] }
        })
      )
      setArtistImages(Object.fromEntries(results.filter(([k,v]) => k && v)))
    }
    fetchArtistImages()
  }, [])'''
            artists_code = artists_code.replace(m.group(1), m.group(1) + inject, 1)
            if 'useEffect' not in artists_code:
                artists_code = artists_code.replace("import { useState }", "import { useState, useEffect }")
            write('src/app/artists/page.js', artists_code)
        else:
            errors.append('artists/page.js: no useState found')
    else:
        skipped.append('artists/page.js: artistImages already present')
else:
    errors.append('src/app/artists/page.js not found')
 
# ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# 3. NAV — reduce gap, add Settings link
# ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
print('[ Nav.js ]')
nav = read('src/app/components/Nav.js')
if nav:
    # Reduce gap
    for old, new in [
        ("gap:'1.5rem'", "gap:'0.75rem'"),
        ("gap: '1.5rem'", "gap: '0.75rem'"),
        ('gap:"1.5rem"', 'gap:"0.75rem"'),
    ]:
        if old in nav:
            nav = nav.replace(old, new)
    # Add Settings link if not present
    if '/settings' not in nav:
        nav = nav.replace(
            "{ href: '/about', label: 'ABOUT' }",
            "{ href: '/about', label: 'ABOUT' },\n    { href: '/settings', label: 'SETTINGS' }",
        )
    write('src/app/components/Nav.js', nav)
else:
    errors.append('Nav.js not found')
 
# ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# 4. GLOBALS.CSS — append card + nav fixes
# ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
print('[ globals.css ]')
CSS_ADDITIONS = '''
 
/* ====== BR DEP XIV additions ====== */
.album-card { display: flex; flex-direction: column; }
.album-card-artist {
  color: #aaa; font-size: 0.85rem;
  white-space: nowrap; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; max-width: 100%;
}
.album-card-title {
  font-weight: 600; white-space: nowrap; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis;

.nav-right { gap: 0.75rem !important; }
'''
append_if_missing('src/app/globals.css', CSS_ADDITIONS, 'BR DEP XIV additions')

      <div style={{ display:'flex', justifyContent:'center',

TERMS = '''
// File: src/app/terms/page.js
export const metadata = { title: 'Terms & Conditions — Banger Ratios' }
export default function Terms() {
  return (
    <div style={{ maxWidth:720, margin:'2rem auto', padding:'0 1.5rem', color:'#ccc', lineHeight:1.7 }}>
      <h1 style={{ color:'var(--pink)' }}>Terms &amp; Conditions</h1>
      <p style={{ color:'#888', fontSize:'0.85rem' }}>Effective: January 1, 2026</p>

      <h2>10. Termination</h2>

      <h2>11. Changes</h2>

    </div>
  )
}

# 8. SETTINGS PAGE — create

print('[ settings/page.js ]')
SETTINGS = '''
// File: src/app/settings/page.js
'use client'
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase'
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation'
 
const INP = { display:'block', width:'100%', padding:'0.6rem 0.8rem',
  background:'#1a1a1a', border:'1px solid #333', color:'#fff',
  borderRadius:4, fontSize:'0.95rem', marginBottom:'0.5rem', boxSizing:'border-box' }
const LBL = { display:'block', color:'#aaa', fontSize:'0.8rem',
  letterSpacing:'0.04em', marginBottom:'0.3rem', marginTop:'1rem' }
const BTN = { background:'var(--pink)', color:'#fff', border:'none',
  padding:'0.55rem 1.4rem', cursor:'pointer', borderRadius:4, fontSize:'0.9rem' }
const CARD = { background:'#0d0d0d', border:'1px solid #222', borderRadius:8,
  padding:'1.5rem', marginBottom:'1.5rem' }
 
export default function Settings() {
  const router = useRouter()
  const [user, setUser] = useState(null)
  const [profile, setProfile] = useState(null)
  const [username, setUsername] = useState('')
  const [displayName, setDisplayName] = useState('')
  const [bio, setBio] = useState('')
  const [spotifyUrl, setSpotifyUrl] = useState('')
  const [appleMusicUrl, setAppleMusicUrl] = useState('')
  const [favAlbums, setFavAlbums] = useState(['','','','',''])
  const [newPw, setNewPw] = useState('')
  const [confirmPw, setConfirmPw] = useState('')
  const [avatarUrl, setAvatarUrl] = useState('')
  const [msg, setMsg] = useState({ text:'', type:'' })
 
  useEffect(() => {
    supabase.auth.getUser().then(async ({ data }) => {
      if (!data?.user) { router.push('/auth'); return }
      setUser(data.user)
      const { data: p } = await supabase.from('profiles').select('*').eq('id', data.user.id).single()
      if (p) {
        setProfile(p)
        setUsername(p.username || '')
        setDisplayName(p.display_name || '')
        setBio(p.bio || '')
        setSpotifyUrl(p.spotify_url || '')
        setAppleMusicUrl(p.apple_music_url || '')
        setAvatarUrl(p.avatar_url || '')
        const fa = Array.isArray(p.favorite_albums) ? p.favorite_albums : []
        setFavAlbums([...fa, ...['','','','','']].slice(0,5))
      }
    })
  }, [])
 
  const flash = (text, type='success') => { setMsg({text,type}); setTimeout(() => setMsg({text:'',type:''}), 3500) }
 
  async function saveProfile() {
    const { error } = await supabase.from('profiles').update({
      username: username.trim(), display_name: displayName.trim(), bio: bio.trim(),
      spotify_url: spotifyUrl.trim(), apple_music_url: appleMusicUrl.trim(),
      favorite_albums: favAlbums.filter(a => a.trim()),
    }).eq('id', user.id)
    flash(error ? 'Error: ' + error.message : 'Saved!', error ? 'error' : 'success')
  }
 
  async function changePassword() {
    if (newPw !== confirmPw) { flash('Passwords do not match', 'error'); return }
    if (newPw.length < 8) { flash('Password must be 8+ characters', 'error'); return }
    const { error } = await supabase.auth.updateUser({ password: newPw })
    flash(error ? 'Error: ' + error.message : 'Password updated!', error ? 'error' : 'success')
    setNewPw(''); setConfirmPw('')
  }
 
  async function uploadAvatar(file) {
    const ext = file.name.split('.').pop()
    const path = user.id + '/avatar.' + ext
    const { error } = await supabase.storage.from('avatars').upload(path, file, { upsert: true })
    if (error) { flash('Upload error: ' + error.message, 'error'); return }
    const { data: { publicUrl } } = supabase.storage.from('avatars').getPublicUrl(path)
    await supabase.from('profiles').update({ avatar_url: publicUrl }).eq('id', user.id)
    setAvatarUrl(publicUrl)
    flash('Photo updated!')
  }
 
  if (!user) return <p style={{ padding:'2rem', color:'#888' }}>Loading...</p>
 
  return (
    <div style={{ maxWidth:640, margin:'2rem auto', padding:'0 1rem' }}>
      <h1 style={{ color:'var(--pink)' }}>Settings</h1>
      {msg.text && <div style={{ padding:'0.75rem 1rem', borderRadius:4, marginBottom:'1rem',
        background: msg.type==='error' ? '#3d0000' : '#003d1a',
        border: '1px solid ' + (msg.type==='error' ? '#cc0000' : '#00aa44'),
        color:'#fff' }}>{msg.text}</div>}
 
      <div style={CARD}>
        <h2 style={{ marginTop:0 }}>Profile Photo</h2>
        <div style={{ display:'flex', alignItems:'center', gap:'1.5rem' }}>
          {avatarUrl ? <img src={avatarUrl} style={{ width:80,height:80,borderRadius:'50%',objectFit:'cover',border:'3px solid var(--pink)' }} />
            : <div style={{ width:80,height:80,borderRadius:'50%',background:'linear-gradient(135deg,var(--pink),#7B2FF7)',
                display:'flex',alignItems:'center',justifyContent:'center',fontSize:'2rem',color:'#fff',fontWeight:700 }}>
                {username?.charAt(0)?.toUpperCase()||'?'}</div>}
          <label style={{ ...BTN, display:'inline-block', cursor:'pointer' }}>
            Upload Photo
            <input type='file' accept='image/*' style={{ display:'none' }}
              onChange={e => e.target.files[0] && uploadAvatar(e.target.files[0])} />
          </label>
        </div>
      </div>
 
      <div style={CARD}>
        <h2 style={{ marginTop:0 }}>Profile Info</h2>
        <label style={LBL}>USERNAME</label>
        <input style={INP} value={username} onChange={e=>setUsername(e.target.value)} placeholder='username' />
        <label style={LBL}>DISPLAY NAME</label>
        <input style={INP} value={displayName} onChange={e=>setDisplayName(e.target.value)} placeholder='Display Name' />
        <label style={LBL}>BIO</label>
        <textarea style={{...INP,height:80,resize:'vertical'}} value={bio} onChange={e=>setBio(e.target.value)} placeholder='About your taste...' />
        <button style={BTN} onClick={saveProfile}>Save Profile</button>
      </div>
 
      <div style={CARD}>
        <h2 style={{ marginTop:0 }}>Favorite Albums</h2>
        <p style={{ color:'#888', fontSize:'0.85rem' }}>Appears at the top of your profile.</p>
        {favAlbums.map((a,i) => (
          <div key={i} style={{ display:'flex', alignItems:'center', gap:'0.5rem', marginBottom:'0.4rem' }}>
            <span style={{ color:'var(--pink)',fontWeight:700,width:20,flexShrink:0 }}>#{i+1}</span>
            <input style={{...INP,marginBottom:0}} value={a}
              onChange={e=>{const arr=[...favAlbums];arr[i]=e.target.value;setFavAlbums(arr)}}
              placeholder={'Favorite #'+(i+1)} />
          </div>
        ))}
        <button style={{...BTN,marginTop:'0.5rem'}} onClick={saveProfile}>Save Albums</button>
      </div>
 
      <div style={CARD}>
        <h2 style={{ marginTop:0 }}>Streaming Links</h2>
        <label style={LBL}>SPOTIFY PROFILE URL</label>
        <input style={INP} value={spotifyUrl} onChange={e=>setSpotifyUrl(e.target.value)} placeholder='https://open.spotify.com/user/...' />
        <label style={LBL}>APPLE MUSIC PROFILE URL</label>
        <input style={INP} value={appleMusicUrl} onChange={e=>setAppleMusicUrl(e.target.value)} placeholder='https://music.apple.com/profile/...' />
        <button style={BTN} onClick={saveProfile}>Save Links</button>
      </div>
 
      <div style={CARD}>
        <h2 style={{ marginTop:0 }}>Change Password</h2>
        <label style={LBL}>NEW PASSWORD</label>
        <input type='password' style={INP} value={newPw} onChange={e=>setNewPw(e.target.value)} placeholder='8+ chars, uppercase, number, symbol' />
        <label style={LBL}>CONFIRM PASSWORD</label>
        <input type='password' style={INP} value={confirmPw} onChange={e=>setConfirmPw(e.target.value)} placeholder='Confirm new password' />
        <button style={BTN} onClick={changePassword}>Update Password</button>
      </div>
 
      <div style={CARD}>
        <h2 style={{ marginTop:0 }}>Privacy</h2>
        <p style={{ color:'#aaa', lineHeight:1.6 }}>
          Your email is never shown publicly. Your ratings are public by default.
          To delete your account, contact us at privacy@bangerratios.com.
        </p>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
'''
write('src/app/settings/page.js', SETTINGS.lstrip())

FRIENDS = '''
// File: src/app/friends/page.js
'use client'
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase'
import Link from 'next/link'
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation'
 
export default function Friends() {
  const router = useRouter()
  const [query, setQuery] = useState('')
  const [results, setResults] = useState([])
  const [following, setFollowing] = useState(new Set())
  const [currentUser, setCurrentUser] = useState(null)
  const [feed, setFeed] = useState([])
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false)
 
  useEffect(() => {
    supabase.auth.getUser().then(({ data }) => {
      if (!data?.user) { router.push('/auth'); return }
      setCurrentUser(data.user)
      loadFollowing(data.user.id)
      loadFeed(data.user.id)
    })
  }, [])
 
  async function loadFollowing(uid) {
    const { data } = await supabase.from('follows').select('following_id').eq('follower_id', uid)
    if (data) setFollowing(new Set(data.map(r => r.following_id)))
  }
 
  async function loadFeed(uid) {
    const { data: fol } = await supabase.from('follows').select('following_id').eq('follower_id', uid)
    if (!fol?.length) return
    const ids = fol.map(r => r.following_id)
    const { data } = await supabase.from('ratings')
      .select('*, profiles(username)')
      .in('user_id', ids)
      .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
      .limit(20)
    if (data) setFeed(data)
  }
 
  async function search() {
    if (!query.trim()) return
    setLoading(true)
    const { data } = await supabase.from('profiles')
      .select('id, username, avatar_url')
      .ilike('username', '%' + query + '%')
      .limit(10)
    setResults(data || [])
    setLoading(false)
  }
 
  async function toggleFollow(targetId) {
    if (!currentUser) return
    if (following.has(targetId)) {
      await supabase.from('follows').delete()
        .eq('follower_id', currentUser.id).eq('following_id', targetId)
      setFollowing(prev => { const s = new Set(prev); s.delete(targetId); return s })
    } else {
      await supabase.from('follows').insert({ follower_id: currentUser.id, following_id: targetId })
      setFollowing(prev => new Set([...prev, targetId]))
    }
  }
 
  return (
    <div style={{ maxWidth:800, margin:'2rem auto', padding:'0 1rem' }}>
      <h1 style={{ color:'var(--pink)' }}>Find Friends</h1>
      <div style={{ display:'flex', gap:0, marginBottom:'2rem' }}>
        <input value={query} onChange={e => setQuery(e.target.value)}
          onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && search()}
          placeholder='Search by username...'
          style={{ flex:1, padding:'0.65rem 1rem', background:'#1a1a1a',
            border:'1px solid #333', borderRight:'none', color:'#fff',
            borderRadius:'4px 0 0 4px', fontSize:'0.95rem' }} />
        <button onClick={search} disabled={loading}
          style={{ background:'var(--pink)', color:'#fff', border:'none',
            padding:'0.65rem 1.1rem', cursor:'pointer', fontSize:'1.1rem',
            borderRadius:'0 4px 4px 0' }}>
          {loading ? '…' : '🔍'}
        </button>
      </div>
      {query && !loading && results.length === 0 && (
        <p style={{ color:'#888' }}>No users found for "{query}"</p>
      )}
      {results.map(u => (
        <div key={u.id} style={{ display:'flex', justifyContent:'space-between',
          alignItems:'center', padding:'0.75rem', border:'1px solid #222',
          marginBottom:'0.5rem', borderRadius:4, background:'#0d0d0d' }}>
          <div style={{ display:'flex', alignItems:'center', gap:'0.75rem' }}>
            {u.avatar_url
              ? <img src={u.avatar_url} style={{ width:36,height:36,borderRadius:'50%',objectFit:'cover' }} />
              : <div style={{ width:36,height:36,borderRadius:'50%',background:'var(--pink)',
                  display:'flex',alignItems:'center',justifyContent:'center',fontWeight:700,color:'#fff' }}>
                  {u.username?.charAt(0)?.toUpperCase()}</div>}
            <Link href={'/profile/' + u.username}
              style={{ color:'#fff', textDecoration:'none', fontWeight:500 }}>
              {u.username}
            </Link>
          </div>
          {currentUser?.id !== u.id && (
            <button onClick={() => toggleFollow(u.id)} style={{
              background: following.has(u.id) ? '#333' : 'var(--pink)',
              color:'#fff', border:'none', padding:'0.3rem 0.9rem',
              cursor:'pointer', borderRadius:3, fontSize:'0.85rem' }}>
              {following.has(u.id) ? 'Unfollow' : 'Follow'}
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      ))}
      {feed.length > 0 && (
        <div style={{ marginTop:'2rem' }}>
          <h2>Friend Activity</h2>
          {feed.map(r => (
            <div key={r.id} style={{ padding:'0.75rem', border:'1px solid #222',
              marginBottom:'0.5rem', borderRadius:4 }}>
              <span style={{ color:'var(--pink)' }}>{r.profiles?.username}</span>
              {' rated a track '}<strong>{r.score}/7</strong>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}
'''
write('src/app/friends/page.js', FRIENDS.lstrip())

print('[ middleware.js ]')
MW = '''
// File: src/middleware.js
import { NextResponse } from 'next/server'
const rateMap = new Map()
export function middleware(request) {
  const ip = request.headers.get('x-forwarded-for') || 'unknown'
  const now = Date.now()
  const windowMs = 60 * 1000
  const maxRequests = 60
  const entry = rateMap.get(ip) || { count: 0, start: now }
  if (now - entry.start > windowMs) { entry.count = 1; entry.start = now }
  else { entry.count++ }
  rateMap.set(ip, entry)
  if (rateMap.size > 5000) {
    for (const [k, v] of rateMap) { if (now - v.start > windowMs * 2) rateMap.delete(k) }
  }
  if (entry.count > maxRequests) {
    return new NextResponse('Too many requests', { status: 429, headers: { 'Retry-After': '60' } })
  }
  return NextResponse.next()
}
export const config = { matcher: ['/api/:path*', '/auth/:path*'] }
'''
write('src/middleware.js', MW.lstrip())

if changed: print(f'Changed ({len(changed)}):', ', '.join(changed))
if skipped: print(f'Skipped ({len(skipped)}):')

if errors: print(f'ERRORS ({len(errors)}):')
for e in errors: print('   !', e)
print()
if errors:
    print('Fix errors above, then re-run: python3 br_patcher.py')
else:
    print('All done! Run: npm run build')

SECTION 3  —  THE ZSH: EVENT NOT FOUND ERROR — EXPLAINED

zsh: event not found: id)   means zsh (your shell) saw the ! or backtick characters inside your grep pattern and tried to interpret them as shell history commands. This is a zsh-specific behaviour.

Why it happens
In zsh, ! inside double-quoted strings triggers history expansion. So grep -n 'emoji|🎵' works fine but any pattern with special characters can trigger it. The autopatcher in Section 2 avoids this entirely because Python does not have this problem.

If you need to run grep manually in zsh
Use single quotes	grep -n 'pattern' file.js   (single quotes are safe)
Escape the !	grep -n "pattern\!" file.js
Disable history expansion	set +H   (run this once, lasts for the session)
Use Python instead	python3 -c "import re,sys; [print(i+1,l.rstrip()) for i,l in enumerate(open('file.js')) if 'pattern' in l]"

-- Add settings columns (safe to re-run)
DO $$ BEGIN
  IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name='profiles' AND column_name='bio')
    THEN ALTER TABLE profiles ADD COLUMN bio text; END IF;
  IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name='profiles' AND column_name='favorite_albums')
    THEN ALTER TABLE profiles ADD COLUMN favorite_albums jsonb DEFAULT '[]'; END IF;
  IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name='profiles' AND column_name='spotify_url')
    THEN ALTER TABLE profiles ADD COLUMN spotify_url text; END IF;
  IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name='profiles' AND column_name='apple_music_url')
    THEN ALTER TABLE profiles ADD COLUMN apple_music_url text; END IF;
  IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name='profiles' AND column_name='display_name')
    THEN ALTER TABLE profiles ADD COLUMN display_name text; END IF;
END $$;
 
-- Allow users to update their own profile
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "update own profile" ON profiles;
CREATE POLICY "update own profile" ON profiles
  FOR UPDATE USING (auth.uid() = id);

 SECTION 1 — Password Settings in Supabase
BR DEP VIII pointed you to Authentication → Policies for password settings. That was wrong — Policies is for Row Level Security. The password strength settings are in a completely different location.

CORRECT LOCATION: supabase.com → your project → Authentication → Auth Providers → Email (not Policies, not Settings)

Step-by-step — finding password settings
1.	Go to supabase.com and log into your project
2.	In the left sidebar, click Authentication
3.	In the Authentication submenu, click Providers (NOT Policies)
4.	You will see a list of providers. Find Email — it should be the first one and already enabled
5.	Click on Email to expand its settings
6.	Scroll down within the Email provider settings
7.	You will see: Minimum password length — set this to 8
8.	Below that: Password Requirements — check these boxes:
•	Require uppercase letters
•	Require lowercase letters
•	Require numbers
•	Require special characters
9.	Scroll to the bottom of the Email provider settings and click Save

IF YOU CANNOT FIND IT: Supabase sometimes moves settings between dashboard versions. If the Email provider does not show password settings, go to Authentication → Configuration → Email Auth. The Minimum password length field will be there.

The client-side password check (already in BR DEP VIII)
In addition to the Supabase setting, the auth/page.js code from BR DEP VIII already validates passwords before they are sent to Supabase. This gives users live feedback as they type. Confirm this code is in your auth/page.js by running:
grep -n 'validatePassword' ~/Desktop/banger-ratios/src/app/auth/page.js
If that command returns nothing, the validatePassword function is missing. Run this to add it:
TERMINAL: UPDATE AUTH/PAGE.JS WITH PASSWORD VALIDATOR
cd ~/Desktop/banger-ratios
cat << 'EOF' > src/app/auth/page.js
// File: src/app/auth/page.js
'use client'
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase'
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation'

function validatePassword(pw) {
  const errors = []
  if (pw.length < 8) errors.push('At least 8 characters')
  if (!/[A-Z]/.test(pw)) errors.push('One uppercase letter (e.g. A, B, C)')
  if (!/[0-9]/.test(pw)) errors.push('One number (e.g. 1, 2, 3)')
  if (!/[!@#$%^&*()_+\-=\[\]{};':"|,.<>\/?]/.test(pw))
    errors.push('One special character (e.g. !, @, #, $)')
  return errors
}

export default function Auth() {
  const router = useRouter()
  const [mode, setMode] = useState('signin')
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('')
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('')
  const [username, setUsername] = useState('')
  const [message, setMessage] = useState('')
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false)

  useEffect(() => {
    supabase.auth.getUser().then(({ data: { user } }) => {
      if (user) router.push('/profile')
    })
  }, [])

  const signIn = async () => {
    if (!email || !password) { setMessage('Please enter email and password.'); return }
    setLoading(true)
    const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({ email, password })
    if (error) { setMessage(error.message); setLoading(false) }
    else { router.push('/profile') }
  }

  const signUp = async () => {
    if (!email || !password) { setMessage('Please enter email and password.'); return }
    const pwErrors = validatePassword(password)
    if (pwErrors.length > 0) {
      setMessage('Password needs: ' + pwErrors.join(' · '))
      return
    }
    setLoading(true)
    const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({ email, password })
    if (error) { setMessage(error.message); setLoading(false); return }
    if (data?.user) {
      await supabase.from('profiles').upsert({
        id: data.user.id,
        username: username || email.split('@')[0],
        email,
      }, { onConflict: 'id', ignoreDuplicates: true })
    }
    setMessage('Account created! Check your email to confirm, then sign in.')
    setLoading(false)
  }

  const onKey = (e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter') mode === 'signin' ? signIn() : signUp() }
  const pwErrors = mode === 'signup' && password.length > 0 ? validatePassword(password) : []

  return (
    <main className="section" style={{ paddingTop: '5rem' }}>
      <div style={{ maxWidth: 440, margin: '0 auto' }}>
        <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', marginBottom: '2.5rem' }}>
          <h1 style={{ fontSize: '2.2rem', fontWeight: 700, marginBottom: '0.5rem' }}>
            {mode === 'signin' ? 'Welcome back' : 'Join Banger Ratios'}
          </h1>
          <p style={{ color: 'var(--gray-text)' }}>
            {mode === 'signin' ? 'Sign in to rate albums.' : 'Create an account to start rating.'}
          </p>
        </div>
        <div style={{ background: 'white', padding: '2.5rem', borderRadius: '20px',
          border: '1px solid var(--border)', boxShadow: '0 4px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.05)' }}>
          <div style={{ display: 'flex', marginBottom: '2rem',
            border: '1px solid var(--border)', borderRadius: '10px', overflow: 'hidden' }}>
            {['signin','signup'].map(m => (
              <button key={m} onClick={() => { setMode(m); setMessage('') }} style={{
                flex: 1, padding: '0.6rem', border: 'none', cursor: 'pointer',
                background: mode === m ? 'var(--pink)' : 'white',
                color: mode === m ? 'white' : 'var(--gray-text)',
                fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.85rem', fontFamily: 'inherit',
              }}>{m === 'signin' ? 'Sign In' : 'Create Account'}</button>
            ))}
          </div>
          {mode === 'signup' && (
            <div style={{ marginBottom: '1rem' }}>
              <label style={{ display: 'block', fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.85rem', marginBottom: '0.4rem' }}>Username</label>
              <input className="input" type="text" placeholder="your_username"
                value={username} onChange={e => setUsername(e.target.value)} onKeyDown={onKey} />
            </div>
          )}
          <div style={{ marginBottom: '1rem' }}>
            <label style={{ display: 'block', fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.85rem', marginBottom: '0.4rem' }}>Email</label>
            <input className="input" type="email" placeholder="you@example.com"
              value={email} onChange={e => setEmail(e.target.value)} onKeyDown={onKey} />
          </div>
          <div style={{ marginBottom: '0.5rem' }}>
            <label style={{ display: 'block', fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.85rem', marginBottom: '0.4rem' }}>Password</label>
            <input className="input" type="password"
              placeholder={mode === 'signup' ? 'Min 8 chars, uppercase, number, symbol' : '••••••••'}
              value={password} onChange={e => setPassword(e.target.value)} onKeyDown={onKey} />
          </div>
          {pwErrors.length > 0 && (
            <div style={{ marginBottom: '1rem' }}>
              {pwErrors.map((err,i) => (
                <p key={i} style={{ color: '#dc2626', fontSize: '0.78rem', marginTop: '0.2rem' }}>✗ {err}</p>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
          {pwErrors.length === 0 && mode === 'signup' && password.length > 0 && (
            <p style={{ color: '#00B84D', fontSize: '0.78rem', marginBottom: '1rem' }}>✓ Password looks good</p>
          )}
          <div style={{ marginBottom: '1.5rem' }} />
          <button onClick={mode === 'signin' ? signIn : signUp} disabled={loading}
            className="primary-btn" style={{ width: '100%', textAlign: 'center', opacity: loading ? 0.7 : 1 }}>
            {loading ? 'Please wait...' : mode === 'signin' ? 'Sign In' : 'Create Account'}
          </button>
          {message && (
            <div style={{ marginTop: '1rem', padding: '0.75rem 1rem', borderRadius: '8px',
              background: message.includes('created') ? '#f0fff4' : '#fff0f5',
              color: message.includes('created') ? '#00B84D' : '#cc0044',
              fontSize: '0.85rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
              {message}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
        <p style={{ textAlign: 'center', marginTop: '1.5rem', color: 'var(--gray-text)', fontSize: '0.82rem' }}>
          By signing in, you agree to help us expose mid albums.
        </p>
      </div>
    </main>
  )
}
EOF

Step 4 — Update NewsBanner.js to use the key
TERMINAL: REPLACE NEWSBANNER.JS WITH LIVE LAST.FM INTEGRATION
cd ~/Desktop/banger-ratios
mkdir -p src/app/components
cat << 'EOF' > src/app/components/NewsBanner.js
// File: src/app/components/NewsBanner.js
'use client'
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'

const FALLBACK = [
  'Kendrick Lamar leads all-time leaderboard with 91% Banger Ratio',
  'Frank Ocean Blonde holds #1 — 96% community score',
  'New: follow friends and see their ratings in real time',
  'Tyler, the Creator IGOR — 93% Banger Ratio from 800+ raters',
  'Chappell Roan rises to 87% — The Rise and Fall of a Midwest Princess',
  'SZA SOS holds at 89% — community favourite for R&B',
  'Rate an album today — contribute to the community leaderboard',
  'New releases added weekly — check the Releases tab',
]

export default function NewsBanner() {
  const [headlines, setHeadlines] = useState(FALLBACK)

  useEffect(() => {
    const key = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_LASTFM_KEY
    if (!key || key === 'your_actual_key_here') return
    fetch(`https://ws.audioscrobbler.com/2.0/?method=chart.gettoptracks&api_key=${key}&format=json&limit=8`)
      .then(r => r.json())
      .then(data => {
        const tracks = data?.tracks?.track || []
        if (tracks.length > 0) {
          const live = tracks.map(t =>
            `Trending: ${t.name} by ${t.artist.name} — rate the album on Banger Ratios`
          )
          setHeadlines([...live, ...FALLBACK.slice(0, 3)])
        }
      })
      .catch(() => {}) // silently use fallback
  }, [])

  const ticker = [...headlines, ...headlines]
  return (
    <div className="news-bar">
      <div className="news-bar-track">
        {ticker.map((h, i) => (
          <span key={i} className="news-bar-item">
            {h}<span className="news-bar-sep">◆</span>
          </span>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
EOF

VS Code fallback — if you prefer: FIRST LINE: // File: src/app/components/NewsBanner.js   LAST LINE: the final closing } of the file. Select all (Cmd+A), delete, paste the content between the first cat line and EOF above.
 SECTION 4 — Fix Git Identity Warning
Your commits are showing: 'Committer: Isaac Lindell <isaaclindell@Isaacs-MacBook-Air.local>'. This means Git is guessing your name and email from your Mac system settings. It works, but the warning is annoying and your commits show the wrong email on GitHub. One command fixes it permanently.

Set your Git identity globally
Run these two commands. Replace the example name and email with your actual ones:
git config --global user.name "James Filmer"
git config --global user.email "you@youremail.com"
Verify it worked:
git config --global --list
You should see user.name and user.email listed. The warning will not appear on your next commit.

OPTIONAL — fix the author on your last commit: git commit --amend --reset-author --no-edit   then   git push --force-with-lease
 SECTION 5 — Correct Build Cache Clear Command
In your terminal output you ran: rm -rf next — this deletes a folder called 'next' which probably did not exist. The correct command has a dot before 'next'. The .next folder (with the dot) is Next.js's build cache. Always use:

# CORRECT — clears the Next.js build cache
rm -rf .next

# WRONG — tries to delete a folder called 'next' (not the cache)
rm -rf next

The dot makes it a hidden folder. You can confirm the build cache exists by running:
ls -la ~/Desktop/banger-ratios | grep .next
If you see a .next folder listed, the cache exists. After running rm -rf .next it will be gone, and npm run dev will rebuild it fresh.

WHEN TO CLEAR THE CACHE: Only clear .next if you see 'weird errors' that do not match your code changes. Most of the time you do not need to clear it — npm run dev watches for changes automatically.

BANGER RATIOS
Complete Deployment & Developer Guide
v5.0 — February 2026
www.bangerratios.com
1. Project Overview
Banger Ratios is a Next.js 16 web application deployed on Vercel, backed by a Supabase PostgreSQL database. Users search any album via the iTunes API, rate tracks 1–7, and the app computes a "Banger Ratio" — the percentage of tracks rated 5 or higher by the community.
Tech Stack
Layer	Technology
Frontend	Next.js 16 (App Router), React 19, Space Grotesk font
Styling	CSS custom properties + Tailwind v4 (utility classes)
Database	Supabase (PostgreSQL) — albums, tracks, ratings, users
Auth	Supabase Auth (email/password)
Music Data	iTunes Search API (free, no key required)
News Feed	Pitchfork RSS via rss2json.com proxy
Hosting	Vercel (auto-deploy from GitHub)
Domain	www.bangerratios.com via Vercel DNS
2. Project Folder Structure
All application code lives inside the src/ directory. Here is what each file does:
File Path	Purpose
src/app/layout.js	Root layout — wraps all pages. Contains NewsBanner + Nav.
src/app/globals.css	All global CSS including design tokens, news ticker animation, nav, buttons, cards.
src/app/page.js	Homepage with hero text, CTA buttons, and animated stat counters.
src/app/components/Nav.js	Sticky navigation. Shows SIGN IN or PROFILE/SIGN OUT based on auth state.
src/app/components/NewsBanner.js	Scrolling news ticker. Fetches Pitchfork RSS. Falls back to curated headlines.
src/app/components/Counter.js	Animated number counter for homepage stats.
src/app/albums/page.js	Browse page. iTunes search dropdown + community-rated albums grid.
src/app/album/[id]/page.js	Individual album rating page. Loads from iTunes API, saves to Supabase.
src/app/artists/page.js	Artists directory. Seeded with top artists. Links to their albums.
src/app/leaderboards/page.js	Ranked albums by Banger Ratio. Podium view for top 3.
src/app/releases/page.js	New releases from iTunes RSS. Filter by genre. Click to rate.
src/app/profile/page.js	User profile. Shows rating stats and history. Redirects if not logged in.
src/app/auth/page.js	Sign in / Sign up form using Supabase Auth.
src/app/merch/page.js	Merch store preview with email waitlist capture.
src/app/about/page.js	Explains the Banger Ratio concept and rating scale.
src/lib/supabase.js	Supabase client. Reads env vars NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL and KEY.
.env.local	Your Supabase credentials. NEVER commit this to GitHub.
next.config.mjs	Next.js config. Allows iTunes image domains (mzstatic.com).
3. Supabase Database Setup
Your Supabase project URL is: https://vqtftxerpwpixhmpowvx.supabase.co
Log in at supabase.com → your project → SQL Editor to run these setup queries.
Required Tables
albums
create table albums (
  id              bigint generated always as identity primary key,
  itunes_collection_id bigint unique,
  name            text,
  artist_name     text,
  artwork_url     text,
  release_date    date,
  genre           text,
  track_count     int,
  banger_ratio    numeric(5,2),
  total_ratings   int default 0,
  created_at      timestamptz default now(),
  updated_at      timestamptz default now()
);
tracks
create table tracks (
  id               bigint generated always as identity primary key,
  album_id         bigint references albums(id) on delete cascade,
  itunes_track_id  bigint unique,
  name             text,
  track_number     int,
  duration_ms      int,
  preview_url      text,
  avg_rating       numeric(4,2),
  total_ratings    int default 0,
  is_banger        boolean default false
);
ratings
create table ratings (
  id         bigint generated always as identity primary key,
  user_id    uuid references auth.users(id) on delete cascade,
  album_id   bigint references albums(id) on delete cascade,
  track_id   bigint references tracks(id) on delete cascade,
  score      int check (score between 1 and 7),
  created_at timestamptz default now(),
  unique (user_id, track_id)
);
Stored Procedure — Recalculate Banger Ratio
This function is called every time a user submits ratings. It updates track stats and recalculates the album's Banger Ratio:
create or replace function recalculate_banger_ratio(p_album_id bigint)
returns void language plpgsql as $$
begin
  -- Update each track's avg rating and banger status
  update tracks t set
    avg_rating = (select avg(score)::numeric(4,2) from ratings r where r.track_id = t.id),
    total_ratings = (select count(*) from ratings r where r.track_id = t.id),
    is_banger = (select avg(score) >= 5 from ratings r where r.track_id = t.id)
  where t.album_id = p_album_id;

  -- Update album banger_ratio and total_ratings
  update albums set
    banger_ratio = (
      select round(
        100.0 * count(*) filter (where is_banger) / nullif(count(*), 0),
      2) from tracks where album_id = p_album_id
    ),
    total_ratings = (select count(*) from ratings where album_id = p_album_id),
    updated_at = now()
  where id = p_album_id;
end;
$$;
Row Level Security (RLS)
Enable RLS so users can only write their own ratings:
alter table albums enable row level security;
alter table tracks enable row level security;
alter table ratings enable row level security;

-- Allow anyone to read albums and tracks
create policy "public read albums" on albums for select using (true);
create policy "public read tracks" on tracks for select using (true);
create policy "public read ratings" on ratings for select using (true);

-- Allow authenticated upserts
create policy "auth upsert albums" on albums for all
  using (auth.role() = 'authenticated') with check (auth.role() = 'authenticated');
create policy "auth upsert tracks" on tracks for all
  using (auth.role() = 'authenticated') with check (auth.role() = 'authenticated');
create policy "own ratings" on ratings for all
  using (auth.uid() = user_id) with check (auth.uid() = user_id);

2. Navigate to the file you want to edit (e.g. src/app/artists/page.js).
3. Click the pencil icon (Edit this file) in the top right.

5. Scroll down to "Commit changes" → write a short message → click "Commit changes".
6. Vercel automatically detects the push and redeploys in ~60 seconds.
7. Visit www.bangerratios.com to see your live changes.

cd ~/Desktop/banger-ratios

npm run dev
Open http://localhost:3000 to preview changes. Edit files in your code editor (VS Code recommended). When ready to deploy:
git add .
git commit -m "describe what you changed"
git push
Vercel auto-deploys. Done.
Option C — Edit directly in Vercel (quick text changes only)
Vercel has a built-in editor for small text changes. Go to vercel.com → your project → Files tab. This is good for quick copy tweaks but not recommended for code changes.
6. How to Customize Each Page
Homepage (src/app/page.js)
Edit the hero headline, subtext, or stat numbers directly in the JSX. The Counter component animates from 0 to whatever value you give it.
To update the stats (Albums Rated, Track Ratings, Active Raters), edit the value={} prop on each Counter component.
Artists Page (src/app/artists/page.js)
The FEATURED_ARTISTS array at the top of the file contains all artist cards. Each artist has:
•	name — Display name
•	genre — Shows under the name
•	ratio — Their Banger Ratio (your editorial call until real data fills in)
•	albums — Number of albums
•	id — iTunes Artist ID (find it by searching artist on iTunes and looking at the URL)
To add an artist, copy one object in the array and fill in the values. To remove one, delete its object.
Albums Page (src/app/albums/page.js)
The SEED_ALBUMS array shows albums as placeholder cards before any community ratings exist. Each has an itunes_id — get this from the iTunes album URL. Once users rate albums, they appear from Supabase automatically.
Releases Page (src/app/releases/page.js)
Fetches the iTunes Top Albums RSS feed live — no editing needed. Genre filter buttons use iTunes genre IDs. To add a genre, add it to the GENRE_IDS object at the top with the correct iTunes ID number.
News Banner (src/app/components/NewsBanner.js)
Tries to fetch Pitchfork RSS news via rss2json.com. If that fails, shows the FALLBACK_HEADLINES array. Edit those strings to control what shows when RSS is unavailable. Ticker speed is controlled by animation: ticker 60s — change 60s to make it faster or slower.
Merch Page (src/app/merch/page.js)
Edit the MERCH array to add, remove, or update products. Each item has name, price, img (emoji), desc, and tag (e.g. "BESTSELLER", "NEW", "COMING SOON"). To connect the email capture to a real service (Mailchimp, ConvertKit), update the Notify Me button onClick handler.
Leaderboard (src/app/leaderboards/page.js)
Fully data-driven — pulls from Supabase automatically. No editing needed. The "This Week" tab filters by albums updated in the last 7 days.
Profile Page (src/app/profile/page.js)
Requires the user to be logged in. Fetches their rating count and recent ratings from Supabase. The profile page redirects to /auth if the user is not signed in.
7. Connecting a Real Music News API
Current Setup — Pitchfork RSS (Free)
The NewsBanner component fetches Pitchfork news via rss2json.com, a free RSS-to-JSON converter. This requires no API key and works immediately. Rate limit is generous for a small site.
Upgrade Option — Spotify or Apple Music API
For richer news (new release announcements, trending artists), you can call the Spotify API:
•	Go to developer.spotify.com and create an app
•	Add SPOTIFY_CLIENT_ID and SPOTIFY_CLIENT_SECRET to Vercel env vars
•	Use the /v1/browse/new-releases endpoint in a Next.js API route
•	Call that API route from NewsBanner.js instead of the RSS feed
The iTunes RSS feed in Releases page (releases/page.js) is completely free, requires no key, and returns real-time Apple Music charts. It is already live.

READ THIS FIRST: Section 1 SQL must be run before any code changes. It fixes the signup crash and creates the follows table. Do not skip it.
 SECTION 1 — Fix Your Database (Run SQL First)
Run every block below in Supabase → SQL Editor → New query → paste → Run → wait for Success. Run them in order. All are safe to re-run if you have already run some.
WHY FIRST: The 'Database error saving new user' crash is caused by a mismatch between the handle_new_user trigger and your profiles table. Block 1 below fixes it. Nothing else will work correctly until this runs.

BLOCK 1 — Fix the signup trigger (fixes 'Database error saving new user')
The existing trigger tries to insert into profiles but the table schema changed when new columns were added. This replaces it with a version that handles all columns safely.
SQL → SUPABASE SQL EDITOR → RUN
-- BLOCK 1: Fix handle_new_user trigger
-- This fixes the 'Database error saving new user' crash on signup.
-- Safe to re-run. Replaces the old trigger with a correct version.

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION handle_new_user()
RETURNS trigger LANGUAGE plpgsql SECURITY DEFINER AS $$
BEGIN
  INSERT INTO profiles (
    id, email, username, created_at,
    banner_url, avatar_url, spotify_id, bio, display_name
  )
  VALUES (
    new.id,
    new.email,
    split_part(new.email, '@', 1),
    now(),
    null, null, null, null, null
  )
  ON CONFLICT (id) DO NOTHING;
  RETURN new;
END;
$$;

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS on_auth_user_created ON auth.users;
CREATE TRIGGER on_auth_user_created
  AFTER INSERT ON auth.users
  FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION handle_new_user();

BLOCK 2 — Add missing profile columns
Adds banner_url, avatar_url, spotify_id, bio, and display_name to the profiles table. Safe to run even if some already exist.
SQL → SUPABASE SQL EDITOR → RUN
-- BLOCK 2: Add social profile columns
DO $$ BEGIN
  IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name='profiles' AND column_name='banner_url')
    THEN ALTER TABLE profiles ADD COLUMN banner_url text; END IF;
  IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name='profiles' AND column_name='avatar_url')
    THEN ALTER TABLE profiles ADD COLUMN avatar_url text; END IF;
  IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name='profiles' AND column_name='spotify_id')
    THEN ALTER TABLE profiles ADD COLUMN spotify_id text; END IF;
  IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name='profiles' AND column_name='bio')
    THEN ALTER TABLE profiles ADD COLUMN bio text; END IF;
  IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name='profiles' AND column_name='display_name')
    THEN ALTER TABLE profiles ADD COLUMN display_name text; END IF;
END $$;

BLOCK 3 — Create the follows table
SQL → SUPABASE SQL EDITOR → RUN
-- BLOCK 3: follows table for friend/follow features
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS follows (
  id bigint GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
  follower_id uuid REFERENCES auth.users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  following_id uuid REFERENCES auth.users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  created_at timestamptz DEFAULT now(),
  UNIQUE(follower_id, following_id)
);
ALTER TABLE follows ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "read follows" ON follows;
CREATE POLICY "read follows" ON follows FOR SELECT USING (true);
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "own follows" ON follows;
CREATE POLICY "own follows" ON follows FOR ALL
  USING (auth.uid() = follower_id)
  WITH CHECK (auth.uid() = follower_id);

-- Enable fuzzy search for username lookup
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS pg_trgm;
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS profiles_username_trgm
  ON profiles USING gin(username gin_trgm_ops);

BLOCK 4 — Create storage buckets for profile images
SQL → SUPABASE SQL EDITOR → RUN
-- BLOCK 4: Storage buckets for avatar and banner uploads
INSERT INTO storage.buckets (id, name, public)
  VALUES ('avatars', 'avatars', true) ON CONFLICT (id) DO NOTHING;
INSERT INTO storage.buckets (id, name, public)
  VALUES ('banners', 'banners', true) ON CONFLICT (id) DO NOTHING;

DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "avatar public read" ON storage.objects;
CREATE POLICY "avatar public read" ON storage.objects
  FOR SELECT USING (bucket_id = 'avatars');
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "avatar owner write" ON storage.objects;
CREATE POLICY "avatar owner write" ON storage.objects FOR ALL
  USING (bucket_id = 'avatars' AND auth.uid()::text = (storage.foldername(name))[1]);

DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "banner public read" ON storage.objects;
CREATE POLICY "banner public read" ON storage.objects
  FOR SELECT USING (bucket_id = 'banners');
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "banner owner write" ON storage.objects;
CREATE POLICY "banner owner write" ON storage.objects FOR ALL
  USING (bucket_id = 'banners' AND auth.uid()::text = (storage.foldername(name))[1]);

BLOCK 5 — Verify everything
SQL → SUPABASE SQL EDITOR → RUN LAST
-- BLOCK 5: Confirm all tables and columns are in place
SELECT table_name, column_name, data_type
FROM information_schema.columns
WHERE table_schema = 'public'
AND table_name IN ('albums','tracks','ratings','profiles','follows')
ORDER BY table_name, ordinal_position;
SUCCESS: You should see 5 tables listed — albums, follows, profiles, ratings, tracks — each with multiple columns. If follows is missing, re-run Block 3.

 SECTION 3 — Password Enforcement
Two parts: the Supabase dashboard setting (server-side) and the client-side validator in auth/page.js that shows live feedback as users type.

Part A — Supabase dashboard setting (correct location)
CORRECT PATH: supabase.com → your project → Authentication → Providers → Email (expand it) → scroll to Password Settings. NOT Policies.

1.	Go to supabase.com → your project
2.	Left sidebar → Authentication
3.	Authentication submenu → Providers
4.	Find Email in the list → click to expand
5.	Set Minimum password length to 8
6.	Check: Require uppercase letters, Require numbers, Require special characters
7.	Click Save at the bottom of the Email provider section

IF YOU CANNOT FIND IT: Try Authentication → Configuration → Email Auth. Supabase occasionally rearranges the dashboard. The Minimum password length field will be in one of these two places.

Part B — Client-side validator in auth/page.js
This shows users exactly what their password is missing as they type, before any server call is made.
TERMINAL: REPLACE AUTH/PAGE.JS
cd ~/Desktop/banger-ratios
mkdir -p src/app/auth
cat << 'EOF' > src/app/auth/page.js
// File: src/app/auth/page.js
'use client'
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase'
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation'

function validatePassword(pw) {
  const errors = []
  if (pw.length < 8) errors.push('At least 8 characters')
  if (!/[A-Z]/.test(pw)) errors.push('One uppercase letter (A–Z)')
  if (!/[0-9]/.test(pw)) errors.push('One number (0–9)')
  if (!/[!@#$%^&*()_+\-=\[\]{};':"|,.<>\/?]/.test(pw))
    errors.push('One special character (! @ # $ ...)')
  return errors
}

export default function Auth() {
  const router = useRouter()
  const [mode, setMode] = useState('signin')
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('')
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('')
  const [username, setUsername] = useState('')
  const [message, setMessage] = useState('')
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false)

  useEffect(() => {
    supabase.auth.getUser().then(({ data: { user } }) => {
      if (user) router.push('/profile')
    })
  }, [])

  const signIn = async () => {
    if (!email || !password) { setMessage('Please enter email and password.'); return }
    setLoading(true)
    const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({ email, password })
    if (error) { setMessage(error.message); setLoading(false) }
    else { router.push('/profile') }
  }

  const signUp = async () => {
    if (!email || !password) { setMessage('Please enter email and password.'); return }
    const pwErrors = validatePassword(password)
    if (pwErrors.length > 0) {
      setMessage('Password needs: ' + pwErrors.join(' · '))
      return
    }
    setLoading(true)
    const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({ email, password })
    if (error) { setMessage(error.message); setLoading(false); return }
    if (data?.user) {
      await supabase.from('profiles').upsert({
        id: data.user.id,
        username: username || email.split('@')[0],
        email,
      }, { onConflict: 'id', ignoreDuplicates: true })
    }
    setMessage('Account created! Check your email to confirm, then sign in.')
    setLoading(false)
  }

  const onKey = (e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter') mode === 'signin' ? signIn() : signUp() }
  const pwErrors = mode === 'signup' && password.length > 0 ? validatePassword(password) : []

  return (
    <main className="section" style={{ paddingTop: '5rem' }}>
      <div style={{ maxWidth: 440, margin: '0 auto' }}>
        <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', marginBottom: '2.5rem' }}>
          <h1 style={{ fontSize: '2.2rem', fontWeight: 700, marginBottom: '0.5rem' }}>
            {mode === 'signin' ? 'Welcome back' : 'Join Banger Ratios'}
          </h1>
          <p style={{ color: 'var(--gray-text)' }}>
            {mode === 'signin' ? 'Sign in to rate albums.' : 'Create an account to start rating.'}
          </p>
        </div>
        <div style={{ background: 'white', padding: '2.5rem', borderRadius: '20px',
          border: '1px solid var(--border)', boxShadow: '0 4px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.05)' }}>
          <div style={{ display: 'flex', marginBottom: '2rem',
            border: '1px solid var(--border)', borderRadius: '10px', overflow: 'hidden' }}>
            {['signin','signup'].map(m => (
              <button key={m} onClick={() => { setMode(m); setMessage('') }} style={{
                flex: 1, padding: '0.6rem', border: 'none', cursor: 'pointer',
                background: mode === m ? 'var(--pink)' : 'white',
                color: mode === m ? 'white' : 'var(--gray-text)',
                fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.85rem', fontFamily: 'inherit',
              }}>{m === 'signin' ? 'Sign In' : 'Create Account'}</button>
            ))}
          </div>
          {mode === 'signup' && (
            <div style={{ marginBottom: '1rem' }}>
              <label style={{ display: 'block', fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.85rem', marginBottom: '0.4rem' }}>Username</label>
              <input className="input" type="text" placeholder="your_username"
                value={username} onChange={e => setUsername(e.target.value)} onKeyDown={onKey} />
            </div>
          )}
          <div style={{ marginBottom: '1rem' }}>
            <label style={{ display: 'block', fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.85rem', marginBottom: '0.4rem' }}>Email</label>
            <input className="input" type="email" placeholder="you@example.com"
              value={email} onChange={e => setEmail(e.target.value)} onKeyDown={onKey} />
          </div>
          <div style={{ marginBottom: '0.5rem' }}>
            <label style={{ display: 'block', fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.85rem', marginBottom: '0.4rem' }}>Password</label>
            <input className="input" type="password"
              placeholder={mode === 'signup' ? 'Min 8 chars, uppercase, number, symbol' : '••••••••'}
              value={password} onChange={e => setPassword(e.target.value)} onKeyDown={onKey} />
          </div>
          {pwErrors.length > 0 && (
            <div style={{ marginBottom: '1rem' }}>
              {pwErrors.map((err,i) => (
                <p key={i} style={{ color: '#dc2626', fontSize: '0.78rem', marginTop: '0.2rem' }}>✗ {err}</p>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
          {pwErrors.length === 0 && mode === 'signup' && password.length >= 8 && (
            <p style={{ color: '#00B84D', fontSize: '0.78rem', marginBottom: '1rem' }}>✓ Password looks good</p>
          )}
          <div style={{ marginBottom: '1.5rem' }} />
          <button onClick={mode === 'signin' ? signIn : signUp} disabled={loading}
            className="primary-btn" style={{ width: '100%', textAlign: 'center', opacity: loading ? 0.7 : 1 }}>
            {loading ? 'Please wait...' : mode === 'signin' ? 'Sign In' : 'Create Account'}
          </button>
          {message && (
            <div style={{ marginTop: '1rem', padding: '0.75rem 1rem', borderRadius: '8px',
              background: message.includes('created') ? '#f0fff4' : '#fff0f5',
              color: message.includes('created') ? '#00B84D' : '#cc0044',
              fontSize: '0.85rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
              {message}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
        <p style={{ textAlign: 'center', marginTop: '1.5rem', color: 'var(--gray-text)', fontSize: '0.82rem' }}>
          By signing in, you agree to help us expose mid albums.
        </p>
      </div>
    </main>
  )
}
EOF

VS Code fallback: FIRST LINE: // File: src/app/auth/page.js   LAST LINE: closing } of the Auth component. Select all, delete, paste content between cat line and EOF.

Part B — Update Nav.js with mobile hamburger menu
TERMINAL: REPLACE NAV.JS
cd ~/Desktop/banger-ratios
mkdir -p src/app/components
cat << 'EOF' > src/app/components/Nav.js
// File: src/app/components/Nav.js
'use client'
import Link from 'next/link'
import { usePathname, useRouter } from 'next/navigation'
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase'

export default function Nav() {
  const pathname = usePathname()
  const router = useRouter()
  const [user, setUser] = useState(null)
  const [menuOpen, setMenuOpen] = useState(false)

  useEffect(() => {
    supabase.auth.getUser().then(({ data }) => setUser(data?.user || null))
    const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange((_e, session) => {
      setUser(session?.user || null)
    })
    return () => subscription.unsubscribe()
  }, [])

  const signOut = async () => {
    await supabase.auth.signOut()
    setUser(null)
    router.push('/')
  }

  const links = [
    { href: '/', label: 'HOME' },
    { href: '/albums', label: 'ALBUMS' },
    { href: '/artists', label: 'ARTISTS' },
    { href: '/leaderboards', label: 'LEADERBOARD' },
    { href: '/releases', label: 'RELEASES' },
    { href: '/friends', label: 'FRIENDS' },
    { href: '/about', label: 'ABOUT' },
    { href: '/merch', label: 'MERCH' },
  ]

  return (
    <nav className="nav">
      <div className="nav-inner">
        <Link href="/" className="logo">
          <span className="logo-square" />
          BANGER <span className="logo-pink">RATIOS</span>
        </Link>
        <div className="nav-right">
          {links.map(({ href, label }) => (
            <Link key={href} href={href} className="nav-link nav-link-desktop">
              <span className={pathname === href ? 'active' : ''}>{label}</span>
            </Link>
          ))}
          {user ? (
            <>
              <Link href="/profile" className="nav-link nav-link-desktop">
                <span className={pathname === '/profile' ? 'active' : ''}>PROFILE</span>
              </Link>
              <button onClick={signOut} className="nav-link-desktop" style={{
                background: 'none', border: 'none', cursor: 'pointer', padding: 0,
                fontFamily: 'inherit', fontWeight: 500, fontSize: '0.82rem',
                letterSpacing: '1.5px', color: 'var(--gray-text)',
              }}>SIGN OUT</button>
            </>
          ) : (
            <Link href="/auth" className="nav-link-desktop">
              <span style={{
                background: 'var(--pink)', color: 'white',
                padding: '0.45rem 1.2rem', borderRadius: '8px',
                fontSize: '0.78rem', fontWeight: 700, letterSpacing: '1px',
                display: 'inline-block',
              }}>SIGN IN</span>
            </Link>
          )}
          <button onClick={() => setMenuOpen(!menuOpen)}
            className="hamburger-btn"
            aria-label="Menu"
            style={{ display: 'none', background: 'none', border: 'none',
              cursor: 'pointer', padding: '0.4rem', marginLeft: '0.5rem' }}>
            <div style={{ width: 22, height: 2, background: 'var(--black)', marginBottom: 5 }} />
            <div style={{ width: 22, height: 2, background: 'var(--black)', marginBottom: 5 }} />
            <div style={{ width: 22, height: 2, background: 'var(--black)' }} />
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
      {menuOpen && (
        <div style={{ background: 'white', borderTop: '1px solid var(--border)',
          padding: '1rem 1.5rem', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: '1rem' }}>
          {links.map(({ href, label }) => (
            <Link key={href} href={href} onClick={() => setMenuOpen(false)}
              style={{ fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.9rem', letterSpacing: '1px',
                color: pathname === href ? 'var(--pink)' : 'var(--black)' }}>
              {label}
            </Link>
          ))}
          {user ? (
            <button onClick={() => { signOut(); setMenuOpen(false) }}
              style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', textAlign: 'left',
                cursor: 'pointer', fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.9rem',
                color: 'var(--gray-text)', fontFamily: 'inherit', padding: 0 }}>
              SIGN OUT
            </button>
          ) : (
            <Link href="/auth" onClick={() => setMenuOpen(false)}
              style={{ fontWeight: 700, color: 'var(--pink)' }}>SIGN IN</Link>
          )}
        </div>
      )}
    </nav>
  )
}
EOF

Part B — Add artwork fetch to albums/page.js
Find the AlbumsContent() function in albums/page.js. Add the following two blocks inside the function, before the return statement. Use VS Code for this one.
VS Code — albums/page.js: FIRST LINE to find: function AlbumsContent()   Find the existing useState declarations near the top of that function, and add the two new blocks below directly after them.

ADD THIS INSIDE ALBUMSCONTENT() — AFTER EXISTING USESTATE LINES
const [seedArtwork, setSeedArtwork] = useState({})

useEffect(() => {
  async function fetchSeedArtwork() {
    const results = await Promise.all(
      SEED_ALBUMS.map(async (album) => {
        try {
          const res = await fetch(`https://itunes.apple.com/lookup?id=${album.itunes_id}&entity=album`)
          const data = await res.json()
          const url = data.results?.[0]?.artworkUrl100?.replace('100x100','400x400')
          return [album.itunes_id, url]
        } catch { return [album.itunes_id, null] }
      })
    )
    setSeedArtwork(Object.fromEntries(results.filter(([,v]) => v)))
  }
  fetchSeedArtwork()
}, [])

Then find the seed card JSX (the div that shows the music emoji). Replace the entire emoji div with:
{seedArtwork[album.itunes_id]
  ? <img src={seedArtwork[album.itunes_id]} alt={album.title}
      style={{ width:'100%',aspectRatio:'1',objectFit:'cover',borderRadius:'10px',marginBottom:'1rem' }} />
  : <AlbumFallback />
}

Part C — Add artist photo fetch to artists/page.js
Same pattern. Find the Artists() component in artists/page.js and add after the existing useState line:
VS Code — artists/page.js: FIRST LINE: export default function Artists()   Add the new state and useEffect after any existing useState lines inside that function.

const [artistImages, setArtistImages] = useState({})

useEffect(() => {
  async function fetchArtistImages() {
    const results = await Promise.all(
      FEATURED_ARTISTS.map(async (artist) => {
        try {
          const res = await fetch(`https://itunes.apple.com/lookup?id=${artist.id}&entity=album&limit=1`)
          const data = await res.json()
          const img = data.results?.[0]?.artworkUrl100?.replace('100x100','300x300')
          return [artist.id, img]
        } catch { return [artist.id, null] }
      })
    )
    setArtistImages(Object.fromEntries(results.filter(([,v]) => v)))
  }
  fetchArtistImages()
}, [])

Then find the gradient avatar div in the artist card JSX and replace it with:
{artistImages[artist.id]
  ? <img src={artistImages[artist.id]} alt={artist.name}
      style={{ width:56,height:56,borderRadius:'50%',objectFit:'cover',marginBottom:'1rem' }} />
  : <div style={{ width:56,height:56,borderRadius:'50%',
      background:'linear-gradient(135deg,var(--pink) 0%,#7B2FF7 100%)',
      display:'flex',alignItems:'center',justifyContent:'center',
      fontSize:'1.4rem',fontWeight:700,color:'white',marginBottom:'1rem' }}>
      {artist.name.charAt(0)}
    </div>
}

// File: src/app/components/NewsBanner.js
'use client'
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'

const FALLBACK = [
  'Kendrick Lamar leads the leaderboard with 91% Banger Ratio',
  'Frank Ocean Blonde holds #1 — 96% community score',
  'New: follow friends and see their ratings in real time',
  'Tyler, the Creator IGOR — 93% Banger Ratio from 800+ raters',
  'Chappell Roan rises to 87% — The Rise and Fall of a Midwest Princess',
  'SZA SOS holds at 89% — community favourite for R&B',
  'Rate an album today — contribute to the leaderboard',
  'New releases added weekly — check the Releases tab',
]

export default function NewsBanner() {
  const [headlines, setHeadlines] = useState(FALLBACK)

  useEffect(() => {
    const key = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_LASTFM_KEY
    if (!key || key === 'YOUR_KEY_HERE') return
    fetch(`https://ws.audioscrobbler.com/2.0/?method=chart.gettoptracks&api_key=${key}&format=json&limit=8`)
      .then(r => r.json())
      .then(data => {
        const tracks = data?.tracks?.track || []
        if (tracks.length > 0) {
          const live = tracks.map(tr =>
            `Trending: ${tr.name} by ${tr.artist.name} — rate the album on Banger Ratios`
          )
          setHeadlines([...live, ...FALLBACK.slice(0,3)])
        }
      })
      .catch(() => {})
  }, [])

  const ticker = [...headlines, ...headlines]
  return (
    <div className="news-bar">
      <div className="news-bar-track">
        {ticker.map((h,i) => (
          <span key={i} className="news-bar-item">
            {h}<span className="news-bar-sep">◆</span>
          </span>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
EOF
