 SECTION 7 — Friends Page (Find & Follow)
Creates src/app/friends/page.js — a page where users search by username, follow others, and see a live feed of what friends are rating. Requires Section 1 Block 3 (follows table) to be done first.

TERMINAL: CREATE SRC/APP/FRIENDS/PAGE.JS
cd ~/Desktop/banger-ratios
mkdir -p src/app/friends
cat << 'EOF' > src/app/friends/page.js
// File: src/app/friends/page.js
'use client'
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase'
import Link from 'next/link'
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation'

export default function Friends() {
  const router = useRouter()
  const [query, setQuery] = useState('')
  const [results, setResults] = useState([])
  const [following, setFollowing] = useState(new Set())
  const [feed, setFeed] = useState([])
  const [me, setMe] = useState(null)
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)

  useEffect(() => {
    async function init() {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser()
      if (!user) { router.push('/auth'); return }
      setMe(user)
      const { data: follows } = await supabase.from('follows')
        .select('following_id').eq('follower_id', user.id)
      const ids = (follows || []).map(f => f.following_id)
      setFollowing(new Set(ids))
      if (ids.length > 0) {
        const { data: activity } = await supabase.from('ratings')
          .select(`score, created_at,
            profiles ( username ),
            tracks ( name ),
            albums ( name, artist_name, artwork_url, itunes_collection_id )`)
          .in('user_id', ids)
          .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
          .limit(20)
        setFeed(activity || [])
      }
      setLoading(false)
    }
    init()
  }, [])

  async function searchUsers(q) {
    if (!q.trim()) { setResults([]); return }
    const { data } = await supabase.from('profiles')
      .select('id, username, email')
      .ilike('username', `%${q}%`)
      .neq('id', me?.id || '')
      .limit(10)
    setResults(data || [])
  }

  async function toggleFollow(userId) {
    if (following.has(userId)) {
      await supabase.from('follows').delete()
        .match({ follower_id: me.id, following_id: userId })
      setFollowing(prev => { const n = new Set(prev); n.delete(userId); return n })
    } else {
      await supabase.from('follows').insert({ follower_id: me.id, following_id: userId })
      setFollowing(prev => new Set([...prev, userId]))
    }
  }

  if (loading) return (
    <div style={{ padding: '5rem', textAlign: 'center', color: 'var(--gray-text)' }}>
      Loading...
    </div>
  )

  return (
    <main className="section">
      <div className="page-header">
        <h1>Find Friends</h1>
        <p>Search for users by username and follow their ratings.</p>
      </div>
      <div style={{ maxWidth: 540, margin: '0 auto 3rem', position: 'relative' }}>
        <input className="input" placeholder="Search by username..."
          value={query}
          onChange={e => { setQuery(e.target.value); searchUsers(e.target.value) }} />
        {results.length > 0 && (
          <div style={{ position: 'absolute', top: '110%', left: 0, right: 0,
            background: 'white', border: '1px solid var(--border)',
            borderRadius: '12px', boxShadow: '0 20px 40px rgba(0,0,0,0.1)', zIndex: 50,
            overflow: 'hidden' }}>
            {results.map(u => (
              <div key={u.id} style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center',
                justifyContent: 'space-between', padding: '0.9rem 1.2rem',
                borderBottom: '1px solid var(--border)' }}>
                <span style={{ fontWeight: 600 }}>
                  {u.username || u.email?.split('@')[0]}
                </span>
                <button
                  onClick={() => toggleFollow(u.id)}
                  style={{
                    padding: '0.4rem 1rem',
                    borderRadius: '8px',
                    border: following.has(u.id) ? '1px solid var(--border)' : 'none',
                    background: following.has(u.id) ? 'white' : 'var(--pink)',
                    color: following.has(u.id) ? 'var(--black)' : 'white',
                    fontSize: '0.82rem', fontWeight: 600, cursor: 'pointer',
                    fontFamily: 'inherit',
                  }}>
                  {following.has(u.id) ? 'Unfollow' : 'Follow'}
                </button>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
      {feed.length > 0 && (
        <div>
          <h2 style={{ fontWeight:700, fontSize:'1.2rem', marginBottom:'1.5rem' }}>
            Friends Activity
          </h2>
          <div style={{ background:'white', border:'1px solid var(--border)',
            borderRadius:'16px', overflow:'hidden' }}>
            {feed.map((r,i) => (
              <Link key={i} href={`/album/${r.albums?.itunes_collection_id}`}
                style={{ display:'flex', alignItems:'center', gap:'1rem',
                  padding:'1rem 1.5rem',
                  borderBottom: i < feed.length-1 ? '1px solid var(--border)' : 'none',
                  textDecoration:'none', color:'inherit' }}>
                {r.albums?.artwork_url && (
                  <img src={r.albums.artwork_url} alt=""
                    style={{ width:44,height:44,borderRadius:'8px',objectFit:'cover',flexShrink:0 }} />
                )}
                <div style={{ flex:1, minWidth:0 }}>
                  <p style={{ fontWeight:600, fontSize:'0.88rem' }}>
                    <span style={{ color:'var(--pink)' }}>{r.profiles?.username}</span>
                    {' rated '}{r.tracks?.name}
                  </p>
                  <p style={{ color:'var(--gray-text)', fontSize:'0.8rem' }}>
                    {r.albums?.artist_name} — {r.albums?.name}
                  </p>
                </div>
                <div style={{ width:36,height:36,borderRadius:'8px',flexShrink:0,
                  background: r.score>=5 ? 'var(--pink)' : '#f0f0f0',
                  display:'flex',alignItems:'center',justifyContent:'center',
                  fontWeight:700,color: r.score>=5 ? 'white' : 'var(--black)' }}>
                  {r.score}
                </div>
              </Link>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
      {feed.length === 0 && following.size === 0 && (
        <div style={{ textAlign:'center', padding:'3rem', color:'var(--gray-text)' }}>
          Search above to find friends and follow their ratings.
        </div>
      )}
    </main>
  )
}
EOF
 SECTION 8 — Profile: Banner, Avatar & Spotify
Upgrades the profile page to Twitter/Instagram style with a wide banner, overlapping avatar photo, and a Spotify connect button. Requires Section 1 Block 4 (storage buckets) to be done first.

Step 1 — Enable Spotify in Supabase (optional)

Step 2 — Add upload functions to profile/page.js
VS Code — profile/page.js: FIRST LINE: export default function Profile()   Add the four functions below inside the Profile() component, before the return statement.

async function uploadFile(file, bucket, suffix) {
  const ext = file.name.split('.').pop()
  const path = `${user.id}/${suffix}.${ext}`
  const { error } = await supabase.storage.from(bucket).upload(path, file, { upsert: true })
  if (error) { console.error(error); return null }
  const { data: { publicUrl } } = supabase.storage.from(bucket).getPublicUrl(path)
  return publicUrl
}

async function uploadBanner(file) {
  const url = await uploadFile(file, 'banners', 'banner')
  if (!url) return
  await supabase.from('profiles').update({ banner_url: url }).eq('id', user.id)
  setProfile(prev => ({ ...prev, banner_url: url }))
}

async function uploadAvatar(file) {
  const url = await uploadFile(file, 'avatars', 'avatar')
  if (!url) return
  await supabase.from('profiles').update({ avatar_url: url }).eq('id', user.id)
  setProfile(prev => ({ ...prev, avatar_url: url }))
}

async function connectSpotify() {
  await supabase.auth.signInWithOAuth({
    provider: 'spotify',
    options: {
      scopes: 'user-read-recently-played user-top-read user-read-private',
      redirectTo: `${window.location.origin}/profile`,
    }
  })
}

Step 3 — Add banner JSX to the top of the return statement
In your profile/page.js, find the return ( statement and add this block as the very first element inside main — before the existing avatar/user div:
{/* Banner — place at the very top of return, inside <main> */}
<div style={{ position:'relative', height:220, background:'#111',

    : <div style={{ width:'100%',height:'100%',
        background:'linear-gradient(135deg,#111 0%,#1a0010 60%,#2d0020 100%)' }} />

  <label style={{ position:'absolute',bottom:'1rem',right:'1rem',

// File: src/app/about/page.js
export default function About() {
  const scale = [
    [7,'Perfect','Would listen on repeat for a week'],
    [6,'Great','Skip nothing — this one delivers'],
    [5,'Good','Solid track, plays well in context'],
    [4,'OK','Would not skip, would not seek out'],
    [3,'Meh','Probably skip on a second listen'],
    [2,'Bad','Drags the album down'],
    [1,'Awful','Should not exist'],
  ]
  return (
    <main className="section">
      <div className="page-header">
        <h1>About Banger Ratios</h1>
        <p>Redefining how music quality is measured — track by track, by the community.</p>
      </div>
      <div style={{ maxWidth:720,margin:'0 auto 4rem',background:'white',
        borderRadius:'20px',border:'1px solid var(--border)',padding:'3rem' }}>
        <h2 style={{ fontWeight:700,fontSize:'1.4rem',marginBottom:'1rem' }}>Why Banger Ratios?</h2>
        <p style={{ color:'var(--gray-text)',lineHeight:1.8,marginBottom:'1rem' }}>
          Streaming numbers reward popularity, not quality. An album can have 10 filler tracks and one
          hit single and still chart at number one. Critic scores reflect one person's opinion.
          Neither tells you what you actually need to know: how many tracks are genuinely worth replaying?
        </p>
        <p style={{ color:'var(--gray-text)',lineHeight:1.8 }}>
          The Banger Ratio answers that. Rate every track 1 to 7. Any track rated 5 or above is a Banger.
          The percentage of Bangers is your Banger Ratio. Simple, community-powered, honest.
        </p>
      </div>
      <div style={{ marginBottom:'4rem' }}>
        <h2 style={{ textAlign:'center',fontWeight:700,fontSize:'1.6rem',marginBottom:'2.5rem' }}>
          The Methodology
        </h2>
        <div style={{ display:'grid',gridTemplateColumns:'repeat(auto-fit,minmax(240px,1fr))',gap:'1.5rem' }}>
          {[
            {num:'01',title:'Rate Every Track',desc:'Score each song 1 to 7. Not the album — every individual track.'},
            {num:'02',title:'Banger Threshold',desc:'A track rated 5 or above is a Banger. Rated 4 or below it does not count.'},
            {num:'03',title:'Calculate the Ratio',desc:'Banger Ratio = (Bangers / total rated tracks) x 100, as a percentage.'},
            {num:'04',title:'Community Average',desc:'All user ratings are averaged per track. Needs 3+ ratings per track for the leaderboard.'},
          ].map((item,i) => (
            <div key={i} className="card">

                {item.num}
              </div>
              <h3 style={{ fontWeight:700,marginBottom:'0.4rem' }}>{item.title}</h3>
              <p style={{ color:'var(--gray-text)',lineHeight:1.6,fontSize:'0.9rem' }}>{item.desc}</p>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style={{ maxWidth:680,margin:'0 auto 4rem',background:'white',
        borderRadius:'20px',border:'1px solid var(--border)',padding:'2.5rem' }}>
        <h2 style={{ fontWeight:700,marginBottom:'1.5rem',fontSize:'1.3rem' }}>The 1–7 Rating Scale</h2>
        {scale.map(([score,label,desc]) => (
          <div key={score} style={{ display:'flex',alignItems:'center',gap:'1rem',
            padding:'0.8rem 0',borderBottom:score>1?'1px solid var(--border)':'none' }}>
            <div style={{ width:36,height:36,borderRadius:'8px',flexShrink:0,
              background:score>=5?'var(--pink)':'var(--bg-soft)',
              display:'flex',alignItems:'center',justifyContent:'center',

              {score}
            </div>
            <div>
              <span style={{ fontWeight:600,fontSize:'0.9rem' }}>{label}</span>
              <span style={{ color:'var(--gray-text)',fontSize:'0.82rem',marginLeft:'0.5rem' }}>— {desc}</span>

      </div>

 SECTION 11 — Git Identity & Build Cache Fix

Correct build cache clear command
# CORRECT — clears Next.js build cache (note the dot)

Pre-push checklist — confirm at localhost:3000
✓	Pink news banner scrolling at top — no emoji, text only
✓	Nav shows all links including FRIENDS and ABOUT
✓	On mobile (or narrow window): hamburger button appears, desktop links hide
✓	Go to /auth → Create Account → weak password → red error messages appear
✓	Strong password (e.g. Banger2024!) → green checkmark appears
✓	Go to /friends — search your own username — you appear in results
✓	Album cards show real artwork (not music emoji) after a 1–2 second load
✓	Artist cards show real photos (or gradient initial as fallback)
✓	npm run build returns no errors

Post-deploy checklist — confirm at www.bangerratios.com
✓	Site loads — no blank screen or crash
✓	Sign up with a new email — no 'Database error saving new user'
✓	After signing up, profile page loads showing your username
✓	Test link preview: opengraph.xyz → paste your URL → preview appears

Your project — quick reference
Item	Value
Local folder	~/Desktop/banger-ratios
Live site	https://www.bangerratios.com
Local test	http://localhost:3000
Supabase	supabase.com → SQL Editor / Authentication / Storage
Password settings	Authentication → Providers → Email → expand → Password Settings
Vercel env vars	vercel.com → banger-ratios → Settings → Environment Variables
Link preview test	https://www.opengraph.xyz
Last.fm API signup	https://www.last.fm/api/account/create
og-image.png location	~/Desktop/banger-ratios/public/og-image.png
Build cache clear	rm -rf .next    (with the dot — NOT rm -rf next)
Start dev server	cd ~/Desktop/banger-ratios && npm run dev
Test before push	npm run build    (must pass before every git push)

Troubleshooting
Problem	Solution
Database error saving new user	Run Section 1 Block 1 SQL — the trigger needs to be updated to include the new profile columns
Friends search shows no results	Confirm Section 1 Block 3 ran (follows table). Also confirm both users have set a username (not blank).
Banner upload fails	Section 1 Block 4 SQL must have run. Check Supabase → Storage — both avatars and banners buckets must exist and be public.
Layout crash (not a React Component)	Run Section 2 terminal command in full. The RootLayout export default function must exist in layout.js.
og-image not showing in preview	File must be named og-image.png in public/ folder. Only visible on live site. Use opengraph.xyz to test.
Last.fm banner showing fallback only	Check .env.local has NEXT_PUBLIC_LASTFM_KEY. Restart npm run dev after editing .env.local (Ctrl+C first).
Mobile nav not working	Confirm Section 4 Part A appended (>>) to globals.css, not replaced (>). Run: tail -30 src/app/globals.css to check.
Password validator not appearing	Confirm validatePassword function is defined before the Auth() component in auth/page.js.
npm run build fails	Read the error — it names the exact file and line. Most common: unclosed JSX tag or missing import.
git push rejected	Run git pull first, then push again.
Vercel deployed but site broken	Add all env vars to Vercel Settings → Environment Variables. Redeploy after adding them.

The order that always works
24.	cd ~/Desktop/banger-ratios
25.	Make your code change
26.	npm run dev → test at localhost:3000
27.	npm run build → confirm zero errors
28.	git add .
29.	git commit -m "describe what changed"
30.	git push
31.	Wait ~60 seconds → check www.bangerratios.com

 SECTION 1 — Fix Your Database (Run SQL First)
Run every block below in Supabase → SQL Editor → New query → paste → Run → wait for Success. Run them in order. All are safe to re-run if you have already run some.
WHY FIRST: The 'Database error saving new user' crash is caused by a mismatch between the handle_new_user trigger and your profiles table. Block 1 below fixes it. Nothing else will work correctly until this runs.

BLOCK 1 — Fix the signup trigger (fixes 'Database error saving new user')
The existing trigger tries to insert into profiles but the table schema changed when new columns were added. This replaces it with a version that handles all columns safely.
SQL → SUPABASE SQL EDITOR → RUN
-- BLOCK 1: Fix handle_new_user trigger
-- This fixes the 'Database error saving new user' crash on signup.
-- Safe to re-run. Replaces the old trigger with a correct version.

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION handle_new_user()
RETURNS trigger LANGUAGE plpgsql SECURITY DEFINER AS $$
BEGIN
  INSERT INTO profiles (
    id, email, username, created_at,
    banner_url, avatar_url, spotify_id, bio, display_name
  )
  VALUES (
    new.id,
    new.email,
    split_part(new.email, '@', 1),
    now(),
    null, null, null, null, null
  )
  ON CONFLICT (id) DO NOTHING;
  RETURN new;
END;
$$;

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS on_auth_user_created ON auth.users;
CREATE TRIGGER on_auth_user_created
  AFTER INSERT ON auth.users
  FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION handle_new_user();

BLOCK 2 — Add missing profile columns
Adds banner_url, avatar_url, spotify_id, bio, and display_name to the profiles table. Safe to run even if some already exist.
SQL → SUPABASE SQL EDITOR → RUN
-- BLOCK 2: Add social profile columns
DO $$ BEGIN
  IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name='profiles' AND column_name='banner_url')
    THEN ALTER TABLE profiles ADD COLUMN banner_url text; END IF;
  IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name='profiles' AND column_name='avatar_url')
    THEN ALTER TABLE profiles ADD COLUMN avatar_url text; END IF;
  IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name='profiles' AND column_name='spotify_id')
    THEN ALTER TABLE profiles ADD COLUMN spotify_id text; END IF;
  IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name='profiles' AND column_name='bio')
    THEN ALTER TABLE profiles ADD COLUMN bio text; END IF;
  IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name='profiles' AND column_name='display_name')
    THEN ALTER TABLE profiles ADD COLUMN display_name text; END IF;
END $$;

BLOCK 3 — Create the follows table
SQL → SUPABASE SQL EDITOR → RUN
-- BLOCK 3: follows table for friend/follow features
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS follows (
  id bigint GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
  follower_id uuid REFERENCES auth.users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  following_id uuid REFERENCES auth.users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  created_at timestamptz DEFAULT now(),
  UNIQUE(follower_id, following_id)
);
ALTER TABLE follows ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "read follows" ON follows;
CREATE POLICY "read follows" ON follows FOR SELECT USING (true);
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "own follows" ON follows;
CREATE POLICY "own follows" ON follows FOR ALL
  USING (auth.uid() = follower_id)
  WITH CHECK (auth.uid() = follower_id);

-- Enable fuzzy search for username lookup
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS pg_trgm;
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS profiles_username_trgm
  ON profiles USING gin(username gin_trgm_ops);

BLOCK 4 — Create storage buckets for profile images
SQL → SUPABASE SQL EDITOR → RUN
-- BLOCK 4: Storage buckets for avatar and banner uploads
INSERT INTO storage.buckets (id, name, public)
  VALUES ('avatars', 'avatars', true) ON CONFLICT (id) DO NOTHING;
INSERT INTO storage.buckets (id, name, public)
  VALUES ('banners', 'banners', true) ON CONFLICT (id) DO NOTHING;

DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "avatar public read" ON storage.objects;
CREATE POLICY "avatar public read" ON storage.objects
  FOR SELECT USING (bucket_id = 'avatars');
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "avatar owner write" ON storage.objects;
CREATE POLICY "avatar owner write" ON storage.objects FOR ALL
  USING (bucket_id = 'avatars' AND auth.uid()::text = (storage.foldername(name))[1]);

DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "banner public read" ON storage.objects;
CREATE POLICY "banner public read" ON storage.objects
  FOR SELECT USING (bucket_id = 'banners');
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "banner owner write" ON storage.objects;
CREATE POLICY "banner owner write" ON storage.objects FOR ALL
  USING (bucket_id = 'banners' AND auth.uid()::text = (storage.foldername(name))[1]);

BLOCK 5 — Verify everything
SQL → SUPABASE SQL EDITOR → RUN LAST
-- BLOCK 5: Confirm all tables and columns are in place
SELECT table_name, column_name, data_type
FROM information_schema.columns
WHERE table_schema = 'public'
AND table_name IN ('albums','tracks','ratings','profiles','follows')
ORDER BY table_name, ordinal_position;
SUCCESS: You should see 5 tables listed — albums, follows, profiles, ratings, tracks — each with multiple columns. If follows is missing, re-run Block 3.

 SECTION 3 — Password Enforcement
Two parts: the Supabase dashboard setting (server-side) and the client-side validator in auth/page.js that shows live feedback as users type.

Part A — Supabase dashboard setting (correct location)
CORRECT PATH: supabase.com → your project → Authentication → Providers → Email (expand it) → scroll to Password Settings. NOT Policies.

1.	Go to supabase.com → your project
2.	Left sidebar → Authentication
3.	Authentication submenu → Providers
4.	Find Email in the list → click to expand
5.	Set Minimum password length to 8
6.	Check: Require uppercase letters, Require numbers, Require special characters
7.	Click Save at the bottom of the Email provider section

IF YOU CANNOT FIND IT: Try Authentication → Configuration → Email Auth. Supabase occasionally rearranges the dashboard. The Minimum password length field will be in one of these two places.

Part B — Client-side validator in auth/page.js
This shows users exactly what their password is missing as they type, before any server call is made.
TERMINAL: REPLACE AUTH/PAGE.JS
cd ~/Desktop/banger-ratios
mkdir -p src/app/auth
cat << 'EOF' > src/app/auth/page.js
// File: src/app/auth/page.js
'use client'
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase'
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation'

function validatePassword(pw) {
  const errors = []
  if (pw.length < 8) errors.push('At least 8 characters')
  if (!/[A-Z]/.test(pw)) errors.push('One uppercase letter (A–Z)')
  if (!/[0-9]/.test(pw)) errors.push('One number (0–9)')
  if (!/[!@#$%^&*()_+\-=\[\]{};':"|,.<>\/?]/.test(pw))
    errors.push('One special character (! @ # $ ...)')
  return errors
}

export default function Auth() {
  const router = useRouter()
  const [mode, setMode] = useState('signin')
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('')
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('')
  const [username, setUsername] = useState('')
  const [message, setMessage] = useState('')
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false)

  useEffect(() => {
    supabase.auth.getUser().then(({ data: { user } }) => {
      if (user) router.push('/profile')
    })
  }, [])

  const signIn = async () => {
    if (!email || !password) { setMessage('Please enter email and password.'); return }
    setLoading(true)
    const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({ email, password })
    if (error) { setMessage(error.message); setLoading(false) }
    else { router.push('/profile') }
  }

  const signUp = async () => {
    if (!email || !password) { setMessage('Please enter email and password.'); return }
    const pwErrors = validatePassword(password)
    if (pwErrors.length > 0) {
      setMessage('Password needs: ' + pwErrors.join(' · '))
      return
    }
    setLoading(true)
    const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({ email, password })
    if (error) { setMessage(error.message); setLoading(false); return }
    if (data?.user) {
      await supabase.from('profiles').upsert({
        id: data.user.id,
        username: username || email.split('@')[0],
        email,
      }, { onConflict: 'id', ignoreDuplicates: true })
    }
    setMessage('Account created! Check your email to confirm, then sign in.')
    setLoading(false)
  }

  const onKey = (e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter') mode === 'signin' ? signIn() : signUp() }
  const pwErrors = mode === 'signup' && password.length > 0 ? validatePassword(password) : []

  return (
    <main className="section" style={{ paddingTop: '5rem' }}>
      <div style={{ maxWidth: 440, margin: '0 auto' }}>
        <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', marginBottom: '2.5rem' }}>
          <h1 style={{ fontSize: '2.2rem', fontWeight: 700, marginBottom: '0.5rem' }}>
            {mode === 'signin' ? 'Welcome back' : 'Join Banger Ratios'}
          </h1>
          <p style={{ color: 'var(--gray-text)' }}>
            {mode === 'signin' ? 'Sign in to rate albums.' : 'Create an account to start rating.'}
          </p>
        </div>
        <div style={{ background: 'white', padding: '2.5rem', borderRadius: '20px',
          border: '1px solid var(--border)', boxShadow: '0 4px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.05)' }}>
          <div style={{ display: 'flex', marginBottom: '2rem',
            border: '1px solid var(--border)', borderRadius: '10px', overflow: 'hidden' }}>
            {['signin','signup'].map(m => (
              <button key={m} onClick={() => { setMode(m); setMessage('') }} style={{
                flex: 1, padding: '0.6rem', border: 'none', cursor: 'pointer',
                background: mode === m ? 'var(--pink)' : 'white',
                color: mode === m ? 'white' : 'var(--gray-text)',
                fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.85rem', fontFamily: 'inherit',
              }}>{m === 'signin' ? 'Sign In' : 'Create Account'}</button>
            ))}
          </div>
          {mode === 'signup' && (
            <div style={{ marginBottom: '1rem' }}>
              <label style={{ display: 'block', fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.85rem', marginBottom: '0.4rem' }}>Username</label>
              <input className="input" type="text" placeholder="your_username"
                value={username} onChange={e => setUsername(e.target.value)} onKeyDown={onKey} />
            </div>
          )}
          <div style={{ marginBottom: '1rem' }}>
            <label style={{ display: 'block', fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.85rem', marginBottom: '0.4rem' }}>Email</label>
            <input className="input" type="email" placeholder="you@example.com"
              value={email} onChange={e => setEmail(e.target.value)} onKeyDown={onKey} />
          </div>
          <div style={{ marginBottom: '0.5rem' }}>
            <label style={{ display: 'block', fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.85rem', marginBottom: '0.4rem' }}>Password</label>
            <input className="input" type="password"
              placeholder={mode === 'signup' ? 'Min 8 chars, uppercase, number, symbol' : '••••••••'}
              value={password} onChange={e => setPassword(e.target.value)} onKeyDown={onKey} />
          </div>
          {pwErrors.length > 0 && (
            <div style={{ marginBottom: '1rem' }}>
              {pwErrors.map((err,i) => (
                <p key={i} style={{ color: '#dc2626', fontSize: '0.78rem', marginTop: '0.2rem' }}>✗ {err}</p>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
          {pwErrors.length === 0 && mode === 'signup' && password.length >= 8 && (
            <p style={{ color: '#00B84D', fontSize: '0.78rem', marginBottom: '1rem' }}>✓ Password looks good</p>
          )}
          <div style={{ marginBottom: '1.5rem' }} />
          <button onClick={mode === 'signin' ? signIn : signUp} disabled={loading}
            className="primary-btn" style={{ width: '100%', textAlign: 'center', opacity: loading ? 0.7 : 1 }}>
            {loading ? 'Please wait...' : mode === 'signin' ? 'Sign In' : 'Create Account'}
          </button>
          {message && (
            <div style={{ marginTop: '1rem', padding: '0.75rem 1rem', borderRadius: '8px',
              background: message.includes('created') ? '#f0fff4' : '#fff0f5',
              color: message.includes('created') ? '#00B84D' : '#cc0044',
              fontSize: '0.85rem', fontWeight: 500 }}>
              {message}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
        <p style={{ textAlign: 'center', marginTop: '1.5rem', color: 'var(--gray-text)', fontSize: '0.82rem' }}>
          By signing in, you agree to help us expose mid albums.
        </p>
      </div>
    </main>
  )
}
EOF

VS Code fallback: FIRST LINE: // File: src/app/auth/page.js   LAST LINE: closing } of the Auth component. Select all, delete, paste content between cat line and EOF.

Part B — Update Nav.js with mobile hamburger menu
TERMINAL: REPLACE NAV.JS
cd ~/Desktop/banger-ratios
mkdir -p src/app/components
cat << 'EOF' > src/app/components/Nav.js
// File: src/app/components/Nav.js
'use client'
import Link from 'next/link'
import { usePathname, useRouter } from 'next/navigation'
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase'

export default function Nav() {
  const pathname = usePathname()
  const router = useRouter()
  const [user, setUser] = useState(null)
  const [menuOpen, setMenuOpen] = useState(false)

  useEffect(() => {
    supabase.auth.getUser().then(({ data }) => setUser(data?.user || null))
    const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange((_e, session) => {
      setUser(session?.user || null)
    })
    return () => subscription.unsubscribe()
  }, [])

  const signOut = async () => {
    await supabase.auth.signOut()
    setUser(null)
    router.push('/')
  }

  const links = [
    { href: '/', label: 'HOME' },
    { href: '/albums', label: 'ALBUMS' },
    { href: '/artists', label: 'ARTISTS' },
    { href: '/leaderboards', label: 'LEADERBOARD' },
    { href: '/releases', label: 'RELEASES' },
    { href: '/friends', label: 'FRIENDS' },
    { href: '/about', label: 'ABOUT' },
    { href: '/merch', label: 'MERCH' },
  ]

  return (
    <nav className="nav">
      <div className="nav-inner">
        <Link href="/" className="logo">
          <span className="logo-square" />
          BANGER <span className="logo-pink">RATIOS</span>
        </Link>
        <div className="nav-right">
          {links.map(({ href, label }) => (
            <Link key={href} href={href} className="nav-link nav-link-desktop">
              <span className={pathname === href ? 'active' : ''}>{label}</span>
            </Link>
          ))}
          {user ? (
            <>
              <Link href="/profile" className="nav-link nav-link-desktop">
                <span className={pathname === '/profile' ? 'active' : ''}>PROFILE</span>
              </Link>
              <button onClick={signOut} className="nav-link-desktop" style={{
                background: 'none', border: 'none', cursor: 'pointer', padding: 0,
                fontFamily: 'inherit', fontWeight: 500, fontSize: '0.82rem',
                letterSpacing: '1.5px', color: 'var(--gray-text)',
              }}>SIGN OUT</button>
            </>
          ) : (
            <Link href="/auth" className="nav-link-desktop">
              <span style={{
                background: 'var(--pink)', color: 'white',
                padding: '0.45rem 1.2rem', borderRadius: '8px',
                fontSize: '0.78rem', fontWeight: 700, letterSpacing: '1px',
                display: 'inline-block',
              }}>SIGN IN</span>
            </Link>
          )}
          <button onClick={() => setMenuOpen(!menuOpen)}
            className="hamburger-btn"
            aria-label="Menu"
            style={{ display: 'none', background: 'none', border: 'none',
              cursor: 'pointer', padding: '0.4rem', marginLeft: '0.5rem' }}>
            <div style={{ width: 22, height: 2, background: 'var(--black)', marginBottom: 5 }} />
            <div style={{ width: 22, height: 2, background: 'var(--black)', marginBottom: 5 }} />
            <div style={{ width: 22, height: 2, background: 'var(--black)' }} />
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
      {menuOpen && (
        <div style={{ background: 'white', borderTop: '1px solid var(--border)',
          padding: '1rem 1.5rem', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: '1rem' }}>
          {links.map(({ href, label }) => (
            <Link key={href} href={href} onClick={() => setMenuOpen(false)}
              style={{ fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.9rem', letterSpacing: '1px',
                color: pathname === href ? 'var(--pink)' : 'var(--black)' }}>
              {label}
            </Link>
          ))}
          {user ? (
            <button onClick={() => { signOut(); setMenuOpen(false) }}
              style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', textAlign: 'left',
                cursor: 'pointer', fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.9rem',
                color: 'var(--gray-text)', fontFamily: 'inherit', padding: 0 }}>
              SIGN OUT
            </button>
          ) : (
            <Link href="/auth" onClick={() => setMenuOpen(false)}
              style={{ fontWeight: 700, color: 'var(--pink)' }}>SIGN IN</Link>
          )}
        </div>
      )}
    </nav>
  )
}
EOF

// File: src/app/components/Icons.js
export function IconMusic({ size = 24, color = 'currentColor' }) {
  return (<svg width={size} height={size} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill={color}>
    <path d="M12 3v10.55A4 4 0 1 0 14 17V7h4V3h-6z"/></svg>)
}
export function IconFire({ size = 24, color = 'currentColor' }) {
  return (<svg width={size} height={size} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill={color}>
    <path d="M13.5.67s.74 2.65.74 4.8c0 2.06-1.35 3.73-3.41 3.73-2.07 0-3.63-1.67-3.63-3.73l.03-.36C5.21 7.51 4 10.62 4 14c0 4.42 3.58 8 8 8s8-3.58 8-8C20 8.61 17.41 3.8 13.5.67z"/></svg>)
}
export function IconTrophy({ size = 24, color = 'currentColor' }) {

const [seedArtwork, setSeedArtwork] = useState({})

useEffect(() => {
  async function fetchSeedArtwork() {
    const results = await Promise.all(
      SEED_ALBUMS.map(async (album) => {
        try {
          const res = await fetch(`https://itunes.apple.com/lookup?id=${album.itunes_id}&entity=album`)
          const data = await res.json()
          const url = data.results?.[0]?.artworkUrl100?.replace('100x100','400x400')
          return [album.itunes_id, url]
        } catch { return [album.itunes_id, null] }
      })
    )
    setSeedArtwork(Object.fromEntries(results.filter(([,v]) => v)))
  }
  fetchSeedArtwork()
}, [])

Then find the seed card JSX (the div that shows the music emoji). Replace the entire emoji div with:

      style={{ width:'100%',aspectRatio:'1',objectFit:'cover',borderRadius:'10px',marginBottom:'1rem' }} />

// File: src/app/components/NewsBanner.js
'use client'
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'

const FALLBACK = [
  'Kendrick Lamar leads the leaderboard with 91% Banger Ratio',
  'Frank Ocean Blonde holds #1 — 96% community score',
  'New: follow friends and see their ratings in real time',
  'Tyler, the Creator IGOR — 93% Banger Ratio from 800+ raters',
  'Chappell Roan rises to 87% — The Rise and Fall of a Midwest Princess',
  'SZA SOS holds at 89% — community favourite for R&B',
  'Rate an album today — contribute to the leaderboard',
  'New releases added weekly — check the Releases tab',
]

export default function NewsBanner() {
  const [headlines, setHeadlines] = useState(FALLBACK)

  useEffect(() => {
    const key = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_LASTFM_KEY
    if (!key || key === 'YOUR_KEY_HERE') return
    fetch(`https://ws.audioscrobbler.com/2.0/?method=chart.gettoptracks&api_key=${key}&format=json&limit=8`)
      .then(r => r.json())
      .then(data => {
        const tracks = data?.tracks?.track || []
        if (tracks.length > 0) {
          const live = tracks.map(tr =>
            `Trending: ${tr.name} by ${tr.artist.name} — rate the album on Banger Ratios`
          )
          setHeadlines([...live, ...FALLBACK.slice(0,3)])
        }
      })
      .catch(() => {})
  }, [])

  const ticker = [...headlines, ...headlines]
  return (
    <div className="news-bar">
      <div className="news-bar-track">
        {ticker.map((h,i) => (
          <span key={i} className="news-bar-item">
            {h}<span className="news-bar-sep">◆</span>
          </span>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

 SECTION 7 — Friends Page (Find & Follow)
Creates src/app/friends/page.js — a page where users search by username, follow others, and see a live feed of what friends are rating. Requires Section 1 Block 3 (follows table) to be done first.

TERMINAL: CREATE SRC/APP/FRIENDS/PAGE.JS
cd ~/Desktop/banger-ratios
mkdir -p src/app/friends
cat << 'EOF' > src/app/friends/page.js
// File: src/app/friends/page.js
'use client'
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase'
import Link from 'next/link'
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation'

export default function Friends() {
  const router = useRouter()
  const [query, setQuery] = useState('')
  const [results, setResults] = useState([])
  const [following, setFollowing] = useState(new Set())
  const [feed, setFeed] = useState([])
  const [me, setMe] = useState(null)
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)

  useEffect(() => {
    async function init() {
      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser()
      if (!user) { router.push('/auth'); return }
      setMe(user)
      const { data: follows } = await supabase.from('follows')
        .select('following_id').eq('follower_id', user.id)
      const ids = (follows || []).map(f => f.following_id)
      setFollowing(new Set(ids))
      if (ids.length > 0) {
        const { data: activity } = await supabase.from('ratings')
          .select(`score, created_at,
            profiles ( username ),
            tracks ( name ),
            albums ( name, artist_name, artwork_url, itunes_collection_id )`)
          .in('user_id', ids)
          .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
          .limit(20)
        setFeed(activity || [])
      }
      setLoading(false)
    }
    init()
  }, [])

  async function searchUsers(q) {
    if (!q.trim()) { setResults([]); return }
    const { data } = await supabase.from('profiles')
      .select('id, username, email')
      .ilike('username', `%${q}%`)
      .neq('id', me?.id || '')
      .limit(10)
    setResults(data || [])
  }

  async function toggleFollow(userId) {
    if (following.has(userId)) {
      await supabase.from('follows').delete()
        .match({ follower_id: me.id, following_id: userId })
      setFollowing(prev => { const n = new Set(prev); n.delete(userId); return n })
    } else {
      await supabase.from('follows').insert({ follower_id: me.id, following_id: userId })
      setFollowing(prev => new Set([...prev, userId]))
    }
  }

  if (loading) return (
    <div style={{ padding: '5rem', textAlign: 'center', color: 'var(--gray-text)' }}>
      Loading...
    </div>
  )

  return (
    <main className="section">
      <div className="page-header">
        <h1>Find Friends</h1>
        <p>Search for users by username and follow their ratings.</p>
      </div>
      <div style={{ maxWidth: 540, margin: '0 auto 3rem', position: 'relative' }}>
        <input className="input" placeholder="Search by username..."
          value={query}
          onChange={e => { setQuery(e.target.value); searchUsers(e.target.value) }} />
        {results.length > 0 && (
          <div style={{ position: 'absolute', top: '110%', left: 0, right: 0,
            background: 'white', border: '1px solid var(--border)',
            borderRadius: '12px', boxShadow: '0 20px 40px rgba(0,0,0,0.1)', zIndex: 50,
            overflow: 'hidden' }}>
            {results.map(u => (
              <div key={u.id} style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center',
                justifyContent: 'space-between', padding: '0.9rem 1.2rem',
                borderBottom: '1px solid var(--border)' }}>
                <span style={{ fontWeight: 600 }}>
                  {u.username || u.email?.split('@')[0]}
                </span>
                <button
                  onClick={() => toggleFollow(u.id)}
                  style={{
                    padding: '0.4rem 1rem',
                    borderRadius: '8px',
                    border: following.has(u.id) ? '1px solid var(--border)' : 'none',
                    background: following.has(u.id) ? 'white' : 'var(--pink)',
                    color: following.has(u.id) ? 'var(--black)' : 'white',
                    fontSize: '0.82rem', fontWeight: 600, cursor: 'pointer',
                    fontFamily: 'inherit',
                  }}>
                  {following.has(u.id) ? 'Unfollow' : 'Follow'}
                </button>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
      {feed.length > 0 && (
        <div>
          <h2 style={{ fontWeight:700, fontSize:'1.2rem', marginBottom:'1.5rem' }}>
            Friends Activity
          </h2>
          <div style={{ background:'white', border:'1px solid var(--border)',
            borderRadius:'16px', overflow:'hidden' }}>
            {feed.map((r,i) => (
              <Link key={i} href={`/album/${r.albums?.itunes_collection_id}`}
                style={{ display:'flex', alignItems:'center', gap:'1rem',
                  padding:'1rem 1.5rem',
                  borderBottom: i < feed.length-1 ? '1px solid var(--border)' : 'none',
                  textDecoration:'none', color:'inherit' }}>
                {r.albums?.artwork_url && (
                  <img src={r.albums.artwork_url} alt=""
                    style={{ width:44,height:44,borderRadius:'8px',objectFit:'cover',flexShrink:0 }} />
                )}
                <div style={{ flex:1, minWidth:0 }}>
                  <p style={{ fontWeight:600, fontSize:'0.88rem' }}>
                    <span style={{ color:'var(--pink)' }}>{r.profiles?.username}</span>
                    {' rated '}{r.tracks?.name}
                  </p>
                  <p style={{ color:'var(--gray-text)', fontSize:'0.8rem' }}>
                    {r.albums?.artist_name} — {r.albums?.name}
                  </p>
                </div>
                <div style={{ width:36,height:36,borderRadius:'8px',flexShrink:0,
                  background: r.score>=5 ? 'var(--pink)' : '#f0f0f0',
                  display:'flex',alignItems:'center',justifyContent:'center',
                  fontWeight:700,color: r.score>=5 ? 'white' : 'var(--black)' }}>
                  {r.score}
                </div>
              </Link>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
      {feed.length === 0 && following.size === 0 && (
        <div style={{ textAlign:'center', padding:'3rem', color:'var(--gray-text)' }}>
          Search above to find friends and follow their ratings.
        </div>
      )}
    </main>
  )
}
EOF

Step 2 — Add upload functions to profile/page.js
VS Code — profile/page.js: FIRST LINE: export default function Profile()   Add the four functions below inside the Profile() component, before the return statement.

async function uploadFile(file, bucket, suffix) {
  const ext = file.name.split('.').pop()
  const path = `${user.id}/${suffix}.${ext}`
  const { error } = await supabase.storage.from(bucket).upload(path, file, { upsert: true })
  if (error) { console.error(error); return null }
  const { data: { publicUrl } } = supabase.storage.from(bucket).getPublicUrl(path)
  return publicUrl
}

async function uploadBanner(file) {
  const url = await uploadFile(file, 'banners', 'banner')
  if (!url) return
  await supabase.from('profiles').update({ banner_url: url }).eq('id', user.id)
  setProfile(prev => ({ ...prev, banner_url: url }))
}

async function uploadAvatar(file) {
  const url = await uploadFile(file, 'avatars', 'avatar')
  if (!url) return
  await supabase.from('profiles').update({ avatar_url: url }).eq('id', user.id)
  setProfile(prev => ({ ...prev, avatar_url: url }))
}

async function connectSpotify() {
  await supabase.auth.signInWithOAuth({
    provider: 'spotify',
    options: {
      scopes: 'user-read-recently-played user-top-read user-read-private',
      redirectTo: `${window.location.origin}/profile`,
    }
  })
}

Step 3 — Add banner JSX to the top of the return statement
In your profile/page.js, find the return ( statement and add this block as the very first element inside main — before the existing avatar/user div:
{/* Banner — place at the very top of return, inside <main> */}

    : <div style={{ width:'100%',height:'100%',
        background:'linear-gradient(135deg,#111 0%,#1a0010 60%,#2d0020 100%)' }} />
  }
  <label style={{ position:'absolute',bottom:'1rem',right:'1rem',
    background:'rgba(0,0,0,0.65)',color:'white',padding:'0.4rem 1rem',
    borderRadius:'8px',cursor:'pointer',fontSize:'0.8rem',fontWeight:600 }}>
    Edit Banner

export default function About() {
  const scale = [
    [7,'Perfect','Would listen on repeat for a week'],
    [6,'Great','Skip nothing — this one delivers'],
    [5,'Good','Solid track, plays well in context'],
    [4,'OK','Would not skip, would not seek out'],
    [3,'Meh','Probably skip on a second listen'],
    [2,'Bad','Drags the album down'],
    [1,'Awful','Should not exist'],
  ]
  return (
    <main className="section">
      <div className="page-header">
        <h1>About Banger Ratios</h1>
        <p>Redefining how music quality is measured — track by track, by the community.</p>
      </div>
      <div style={{ maxWidth:720,margin:'0 auto 4rem',background:'white',
        borderRadius:'20px',border:'1px solid var(--border)',padding:'3rem' }}>
        <h2 style={{ fontWeight:700,fontSize:'1.4rem',marginBottom:'1rem' }}>Why Banger Ratios?</h2>
        <p style={{ color:'var(--gray-text)',lineHeight:1.8,marginBottom:'1rem' }}>
          Streaming numbers reward popularity, not quality. An album can have 10 filler tracks and one
          hit single and still chart at number one. Critic scores reflect one person's opinion.
          Neither tells you what you actually need to know: how many tracks are genuinely worth replaying?
        </p>
        <p style={{ color:'var(--gray-text)',lineHeight:1.8 }}>
          The Banger Ratio answers that. Rate every track 1 to 7. Any track rated 5 or above is a Banger.
          The percentage of Bangers is your Banger Ratio. Simple, community-powered, honest.
        </p>
      </div>
      <div style={{ marginBottom:'4rem' }}>
        <h2 style={{ textAlign:'center',fontWeight:700,fontSize:'1.6rem',marginBottom:'2.5rem' }}>
          The Methodology
        </h2>
        <div style={{ display:'grid',gridTemplateColumns:'repeat(auto-fit,minmax(240px,1fr))',gap:'1.5rem' }}>
          {[
            {num:'01',title:'Rate Every Track',desc:'Score each song 1 to 7. Not the album — every individual track.'},
            {num:'02',title:'Banger Threshold',desc:'A track rated 5 or above is a Banger. Rated 4 or below it does not count.'},
            {num:'03',title:'Calculate the Ratio',desc:'Banger Ratio = (Bangers / total rated tracks) x 100, as a percentage.'},

            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>

        borderRadius:'20px',border:'1px solid var(--border)',padding:'2.5rem' }}>
        <h2 style={{ fontWeight:700,marginBottom:'1.5rem',fontSize:'1.3rem' }}>The 1–7 Rating Scale</h2>

          <div key={score} style={{ display:'flex',alignItems:'center',gap:'1rem',
            padding:'0.8rem 0',borderBottom:score>1?'1px solid var(--border)':'none' }}>
            <div style={{ width:36,height:36,borderRadius:'8px',flexShrink:0,

        borderRadius:'20px',padding:'3rem',color:'white' }}>

}

 SECTION 11 — Git Identity & Build Cache Fix

Fix Git identity warning
Run these two commands once. Replace the example values with your actual name and email:
git config --global user.name "jamestfilmer-ops"
git config --global user.email "jamestfilmer@gmail.com"

# Verify
git config --global --list

Correct build cache clear command
# CORRECT — clears Next.js build cache (note the dot)
rm -rf .next

# WRONG — tries to delete a folder called 'next' (no dot)
rm -rf next

WHEN TO USE IT: Only clear .next when you see errors that don't match your code. Normal development does not require clearing it.
 SECTION 12 — Final Push & Cheat Sheet

Push everything
cd ~/Desktop/banger-ratios
npm run build
# Must show: Compiled successfully — fix any errors before next step

git add .
git commit -m "BR DEP XI: all features deployed"
git push
# Wait ~60 seconds then check www.bangerratios.com

Pre-push checklist — confirm at localhost:3000
✓	Pink news banner scrolling at top — no emoji, text only
✓	Nav shows all links including FRIENDS and ABOUT
✓	On mobile (or narrow window): hamburger button appears, desktop links hide
✓	Go to /auth → Create Account → weak password → red error messages appear
✓	Strong password (e.g. Banger2024!) → green checkmark appears
✓	Go to /friends — search your own username — you appear in results
✓	Album cards show real artwork (not music emoji) after a 1–2 second load
✓	Artist cards show real photos (or gradient initial as fallback)
✓	npm run build returns no errors

Post-deploy checklist — confirm at www.bangerratios.com
✓	Site loads — no blank screen or crash
✓	Sign up with a new email — no 'Database error saving new user'
✓	After signing up, profile page loads showing your username
✓	Test link preview: opengraph.xyz → paste your URL → preview appears

Your project — quick reference
Item	Value
Local folder	~/Desktop/banger-ratios
Live site	https://www.bangerratios.com
Local test	http://localhost:3000
Supabase	supabase.com → SQL Editor / Authentication / Storage
Password settings	Authentication → Providers → Email → expand → Password Settings
Vercel env vars	vercel.com → banger-ratios → Settings → Environment Variables
Link preview test	https://www.opengraph.xyz
Last.fm API signup	https://www.last.fm/api/account/create
og-image.png location	~/Desktop/banger-ratios/public/og-image.png
Build cache clear	rm -rf .next    (with the dot — NOT rm -rf next)
Start dev server	cd ~/Desktop/banger-ratios && npm run dev
Test before push	npm run build    (must pass before every git push)

Troubleshooting
Problem	Solution
Database error saving new user	Run Section 1 Block 1 SQL — the trigger needs to be updated to include the new profile columns
Friends search shows no results	Confirm Section 1 Block 3 ran (follows table). Also confirm both users have set a username (not blank).
Banner upload fails	Section 1 Block 4 SQL must have run. Check Supabase → Storage — both avatars and banners buckets must exist and be public.
Layout crash (not a React Component)	Run Section 2 terminal command in full. The RootLayout export default function must exist in layout.js.
og-image not showing in preview	File must be named og-image.png in public/ folder. Only visible on live site. Use opengraph.xyz to test.
Last.fm banner showing fallback only	Check .env.local has NEXT_PUBLIC_LASTFM_KEY. Restart npm run dev after editing .env.local (Ctrl+C first).
Mobile nav not working	Confirm Section 4 Part A appended (>>) to globals.css, not replaced (>). Run: tail -30 src/app/globals.css to check.
Password validator not appearing	Confirm validatePassword function is defined before the Auth() component in auth/page.js.
npm run build fails	Read the error — it names the exact file and line. Most common: unclosed JSX tag or missing import.
git push rejected	Run git pull first, then push again.
Vercel deployed but site broken	Add all env vars to Vercel Settings → Environment Variables. Redeploy after adding them.

The order that always works
24.	cd ~/Desktop/banger-ratios
25.	Make your code change
26.	npm run dev → test at localhost:3000
27.	npm run build → confirm zero errors
28.	git add .
29.	git commit -m "describe what changed"
30.	git push
31.	Wait ~60 seconds → check www.bangerratios.com
